nārāyaṇam namaskṛtya naram ca eva narottamam lomaharṣaṇa putraḥ ugraśravāḥ sūtaḥ paurāṇikaḥ naimiṣa araṇye śaunakasya kula pateḥ dvādaśa vārṣike satre samāsīnān abhyagacchat brahmarṣīn saṃśita vratān vinaya avanataḥ bhūtvā kadā cit sūtanandanaḥ tam āśramam anuprāptam naimiṣa araṇya vāsinaḥ abhivādya munīn tān tu sarvān eva kṛtāñjaliḥ atha teṣu upaviṣṭeṣu sarveṣu eva tapasviṣu nirdiṣṭam āsanam bheje vinayāt lomaharṣaṇiḥ sukha āsīnam tatas tam tu viśrāntam upalakṣya ca athā apṛcchat ṛṣiḥ tatra kaḥ cit prastāvayan kathāḥ kālaḥ kamala patra akṣa śaṃsa etat pṛcchataḥ mama sūtaḥ uvāca kṛṣṇadvaipāyana proktāḥ su puṇyāḥ vividhāḥ kathāḥ kathitāḥ ca api vidhivat yāḥ vaiśaṃpāyanena vai śrutvā aham tāḥ vicitra arthāḥ mahābhārata saṃśritāḥ bahūni saṃparikramya tīrthāni āyatanāni ca samantapañcakam nāma puṇyam dvija niṣevitam gatavān asmi tam deśam yuddham yatra abhavat purā pāṇḍavānām kurūṇām ca sarveṣām ca mahīkṣitām didṛkṣuḥ āgataḥ tasmāt samīpam bhavatām iha āyuṣmantaḥ sarve eva brahma bhūtāḥ hi me matāḥ asmin yajñe mahābhāgāḥ sūrya pāvaka varcasaḥ kṛta abhiṣekāḥ śucayaḥ kṛta japyāḥ huta agnayaḥ bhavantaḥ āsate svasthāḥ bravīmi kim aham dvijāḥ purāṇa saṃśritāḥ puṇyāḥ kathāḥ vā dharma saṃśritāḥ itivṛttam narendrāṇām ṛṣīṇām ca mahātmanām ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ dvaipāyanena yat proktam purāṇam parama ṛṣiṇā sūkṣma artha nyāya yuktasya veda arthaiḥ bhūṣitasya ca bhāratasya itihāsasya puṇyām grantha artha saṃyutām saṃskāra upagatām brāhmīm nānā śāstra upabṛṃhitām janamejayasya yām rājñaḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uktavān yathāvat saḥ ṛṣiḥ tuṣṭyā satre dvaipāyana ājñayā vedaiḥ caturbhiḥ samitām vyāsasya adbhuta karmaṇaḥ saṃhitām śrotum icchāmaḥ dharmyām pāpa bhaya apahām sūtaḥ uvāca ādyam puruṣam īśānam puruhūtam puruṣṭutam ṛtam ekākṣaram brahma vyakta avyaktam sanātanam parāvarāṇām sraṣṭāram purāṇam param avyayam maṅgalyam maṅgalam viṣṇum vareṇyam anagham śucim namaskṛtya hṛṣīkeśam carācara gurum harim pravakṣyāmi matam kṛtsnam vyāsasya amita tejasaḥ ācakhyuḥ kavayaḥ ke cit saṃprati ācakṣate pare idam tu triṣu lokeṣu mahat jñānam pratiṣṭhitam alaṃkṛtam śubhaiḥ śabdaiḥ samayaiḥ divya mānuṣaiḥ bṛhat aṇḍam abhūt ekam prajānām bījam akṣayam avyaktam kāraṇam sūkṣmam yat tat sat asat ātmakam yasmāt pitāmahaḥ jajñe prabhuḥ ekaḥ prajāpatiḥ brahmā sura guruḥ sthāṇuḥ manuḥ kaḥ parameṣṭhī atha prācetasaḥ tathā dakṣaḥ dakṣa putrāḥ ca sapta ye tatas prajānām patayaḥ prābhavan ekaviṃśatiḥ puruṣaḥ ca aprameya ātmā yam sarvam ṛṣayaḥ viduḥ viśvedevāḥ tathā ādityāḥ vasavaḥ atha aśvinau api yakṣāḥ sādhyāḥ piśācāḥ ca guhyakāḥ pitaraḥ tathā tatas prasūtāḥ vidvāṃsaḥ śiṣṭāḥ brahmarṣayaḥ amalāḥ rājarṣayaḥ ca bahavaḥ sarvaiḥ samuditāḥ guṇaiḥ āpaḥ dyauḥ pṛthivī vāyuḥ antarikṣam diśaḥ tathā saṃvatsara ṛtavaḥ māsāḥ pakṣa ahar rātrayaḥ kramāt yat ca anyat api tat sarvam saṃbhūtam loka sākṣikam yat idam dṛśyate kim cit bhūtam sthāvara jaṅgamam yathā ṛtau ṛtu liṅgāni nānā rūpāṇi paryaye dṛśyante tāni tāni eva tathā bhāvāḥ yuga ādiṣu evam etat anādi antam bhūta saṃhāra kārakam trayastriṃśat sahasrāṇi trayastriṃśat śatāni ca trayastriṃśat ca devānām sṛṣṭiḥ saṃkṣepa lakṣaṇā divasputraḥ bṛhadbhānuḥ cakṣuḥ ātmā vibhāvasuḥ savitā ca ṛcīkaḥ arkaḥ bhānuḥ āśāvahaḥ raviḥ putrāḥ vivasvataḥ sarve mahyaḥ teṣām tathā avaraḥ devabhrāj tanayaḥ tasya tasmāt subhrāj iti smṛtaḥ subhrājaḥ tu trayaḥ putrāḥ prajāvantaḥ bahu śrutāḥ daśajyotiḥ śatajyotiḥ sahasrajyotiḥ ātmavān daśa putra sahasrāṇi daśajyoteḥ mahātmanaḥ tatas daśaguṇāḥ ca anye śatajyoteḥ iha ātmajāḥ bhūyas tatas daśaguṇāḥ sahasrajyotiṣaḥ sutāḥ tebhyaḥ ayam kuru vaṃśaḥ ca yadūnām bharatasya ca yayāti ikṣvāku vaṃśaḥ ca rājarṣīṇām ca sarvaśas saṃbhūtāḥ bahavaḥ vaṃśāḥ bhūta sargāḥ sa vistarāḥ bhūta sthānāni sarvāṇi rahasyam trividham ca yat veda yogam sa vijñānam dharmaḥ arthaḥ kāmaḥ eva ca dharma kāma artha śāstrāṇi śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca lokayātrā vidhānam ca saṃbhūtam dṛṣṭavān ṛṣiḥ itihāsāḥ sa vaiyākhyāḥ vividhāḥ śrutayaḥ api ca vistīrya etat mahat jñānam ṛṣiḥ saṃkṣepam abravīt iṣṭam hi viduṣām loke samāsa vyāsa dhāraṇam manu ādi bhāratam ke cid āstīka ādi tathā apare vividham saṃhitā jñānam dīpayanti manīṣiṇaḥ vyākhyātum kuśalāḥ ke cid grantham dhārayitum pare itihāsam imam cakre puṇyam satyavatī sutaḥ parāśara ātmajaḥ vidvān brahmarṣiḥ saṃśita vrataḥ mātuḥ niyogāt dharma ātmā gāṅgeyasya ca dhīmataḥ kṣetre vicitra vīryasya kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ purā trīn agnīn iva kauravyān janayām āsa vīryavān utpādya dhṛtarāṣṭram ca pāṇḍum viduram eva ca jagāma tapase dhīmān punar eva āśramam prati teṣu jāteṣu vṛddheṣu gateṣu paramām gatim abravīt bhāratam loke mānuṣe asmin mahān ṛṣiḥ janamejayena pṛṣṭaḥ san brāhmaṇaiḥ ca sahasraśas śaśāsa śiṣyam āsīnam vaiśaṃpāyanam antike sa sadasyaiḥ saha āsīnaḥ śrāvayām āsa bhāratam karma antareṣu yajñasya codyamānaḥ punar punar vistaram kuru vaṃśasya gāndhāryāḥ dharma śīla tām kṣattuḥ prajñām dhṛtim kuntyāḥ samyak dvaipāyanaḥ abravīt vāsudevasya māhātmyam pāṇḍavānām ca satyatām durvṛttam dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām uktavān bhagavān ṛṣiḥ caturviṃśati sāhasrīm cakre bhārata saṃhitām upākhyānaiḥ vinā tāvat bhāratam procyate budhaiḥ tatas adhyardha śatam bhūyas saṃkṣepam kṛtavān ṛṣiḥ anukramaṇim adhyāyam vṛttāntānām sa parvaṇām nāradaḥ aśrāvayat devān asitaḥ devalaḥ pitṝn gandharva yakṣa rakṣāṃsi śrāvayām āsa vai śukaḥ duryodhanaḥ manyu mayaḥ mahā drumaḥ skandhaḥ karṇaḥ śakuniḥ tasya śākhāḥ duḥśāsanaḥ puṣpa phale samṛddhe mūlam rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ amanīṣī mādrī sutau puṣpa phale samṛddhe mūlam kṛṣṇaḥ brahma ca brāhmaṇāḥ ca pāṇḍuḥ jitvā bahūn deśān yudhā vikramaṇena ca araṇye mṛgayā śīlaḥ nyavasat sa janaḥ tadā mṛga vyavāya nidhane kṛcchrām prāpa saḥ āpadam janma prabhṛti pārthānām tatra ācāra vidhi kramaḥ dharmasya vāyoḥ śakrasya devayoḥ ca tathā aśvinoḥ tāpasaiḥ saha saṃvṛddhāḥ mātṛbhyām parirakṣitāḥ medhya araṇyeṣu puṇyeṣu mahatām āśrameṣu ca ṛṣibhiḥ ca tadā ānītāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān prati svayam śiśavaḥ ca abhirūpāḥ ca jaṭilāḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ putrāḥ ca bhrātaraḥ ca ime śiṣyāḥ ca suhṛdaḥ ca vaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ete iti uktvā munayaḥ antarhitāḥ tatas tān taiḥ niveditān dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavān kauravāḥ tadā śiṣṭāḥ ca varṇāḥ paurāḥ ye te harṣāt cukruśuḥ bhṛśam yadā cira mṛtaḥ pāṇḍuḥ katham tasya iti ca apare svāgatam sarvathā diṣṭyā pāṇḍoḥ paśyāma saṃtatim ucyatām svāgatam iti vācaḥ aśrūyanta sarvaśas antarhitānām bhūtānām nisvanaḥ tumulaḥ abhavat puṣpa vṛṣṭiḥ śubhāḥ gandhāḥ śaṅkha dundubhi nisvanāḥ āsan praveśe pārthānām tat adbhutam iva abhavat tad prītyā ca eva sarveṣām paurāṇām harṣa saṃbhavaḥ śabdaḥ āsīt mahān tatra diva spṛś kīrti vardhanaḥ te api adhītya akhilān vedān śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca nyavasan pāṇḍavāḥ tatra pūjitāḥ akutobhayāḥ yudhiṣṭhirasya śaucena prītāḥ prakṛtayaḥ abhavan guru śuśrūṣayā kuntyāḥ yamayoḥ vinayena ca tutoṣa lokaḥ sakalaḥ teṣām śaurya guṇena ca samavāye tatas rājñām kanyām bhartṛ svayaṃvarām prāptavān arjunaḥ kṛṣṇām kṛtvā karma su duṣkaram ādityaḥ iva duṣprekṣyaḥ samareṣu api ca abhavat sa sarvān pārthivān jitvā sarvān ca mahataḥ gaṇān ājahāra arjunaḥ rājñe rājasūyam mahā kratum annavān dakṣiṇāvān ca sarvaiḥ samuditaḥ guṇaiḥ yudhiṣṭhireṇa saṃprāptaḥ rājasūyaḥ mahā kratuḥ maṇi kāñcana ratnāni go hasti aśva dhanāni ca samṛddhām tām tathā dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānām tadā śriyam īrṣyā samutthaḥ su mahān tasya manyuḥ ajāyata vimāna pratimām ca api mayena su kṛtām sabhām pāṇḍavānām upahṛtām sa dṛṣṭvā paryatapyata pratyakṣam vāsudevasya bhīmena an abhijāta vat kathitaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya vivarṇaḥ hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ anvajānāt tatas dyūtam dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ suta priyaḥ na ati prīta manāḥ ca āsīt vivādān ca anvamodata dyūta ādīn anayān ghorān pravṛddhān ca api upaikṣata nirasya viduram droṇam bhīṣmam śāradvatam kṛpam jayatsu pāṇḍu putreṣu śrutvā su mahat apriyam duryodhana matam jñātvā karṇasya śakuneḥ tathā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ciram dhyātvā saṃjayam vākyam abravīt śṛṇu saṃjaya me sarvam na me asūyitum arhasi śrutavān asi medhāvī buddhimān prājña saṃmataḥ na me viśeṣaḥ putreṣu sveṣu pāṇḍu suteṣu ca vṛddham mām abhyasūyanti putrāḥ manyu parāyaṇāḥ aham tu acakṣuḥ kārpaṇyāt putra prītyā sahāmi tat rājasūye śriyam dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavasya mahā ojasaḥ tat ca avahasanam prāpya sabhā rohaṇa darśane amarṣitaḥ svayam jetum aśaktaḥ pāṇḍavān raṇe nirutsāhaḥ ca saṃprāptum śriyam a kṣatriyaḥ yathā tatra yat yat yathā jñātam mayā saṃjaya tat śṛṇu śrutvā hi mama vākyāni buddhyā yuktāni tattvataḥ tatas jñāsyasi mām saute prajñā cakṣuṣam iti uta yadā aśrauṣam dhanuḥ āyamya citram viddham lakṣyam pātitam vai pṛthivyām kṛṣṇām hṛtām paśyatām sarva rājñām tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam dvārakāyām subhadrām prasahya ūḍhām mādhavīm arjunena indraprastham vṛṣṇi vīrau ca yātau tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam devarājam pravṛṣṭam śaraiḥ divyaiḥ vāritam ca arjunena agnim tathā tarpitam khāṇḍave ca tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam hṛta rājyam yudhiṣṭhiram parājitam saubalena akṣavatyām anvāgatam bhrātṛbhiḥ aprameyaiḥ tadā nā āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam draupadīm aśru kaṇṭhīm sabhām nītām duḥkhitām eka vastrām rajasvalām nāthavatīm anātha vat yadā aśrauṣam vividhāḥ tāta ceṣṭāḥ dharma ātmanām prasthitānām vanāya jyeṣṭha prītyā kliśyatām pāṇḍavānām tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam snātakānām sahasraiḥ anvāgatam dharmarājam vanastham bhikṣā bhujām brāhmaṇānām mahātmanām tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam arjunaḥ devadevam kirāta rūpam tryambakam toṣya yuddhe avāpa tat pāśupatam mahā astram tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam tridiva stham dhanaṃjayam śakrāt sākṣāt divyam astram yathāvat adhīyānam śaṃsitam satya saṃdham tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vaiśravaṇena sārdham samāgatam bhīmam anyān ca pārthān tasmin deśe mānuṣāṇām agamye tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam ghoṣa yātrā gatānām bandham gandharvaiḥ mokṣaṇam ca arjunena sveṣām sutānām karṇa buddhau ratānām tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam yakṣa rūpeṇa dharmam samāgatam dharmarājena sūta praśnān uktān vibruvantam ca samyak yadā aśrauṣam māmakānām variṣṭhān dhanaṃjayena eka rathena bhagnān virāṭa rāṣṭre vasatā mahātmanā tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam satkṛtām matsya rājñā sutām dattām uttarām arjunāya tām ca arjunaḥ pratyagṛhṇāt suta arthe tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya akṣauhiṇīḥ sapta yudhiṣṭhirasya tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam nara nārāyaṇau tau kṛṣṇa arjunau vadataḥ nāradasya aham draṣṭā brahma loke sadā iti tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam mādhavam vāsudevam sarva ātmanā pāṇḍava arthe niviṣṭam yasya imām gām vikramam ekam āhuḥ tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam karṇa duryodhanābhyām buddhim kṛtām nigrahe keśavasya tam ca ātmānam bahudhā darśayānam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vāsudeve prayāte rathasya ekām agratas tiṣṭhamānām ārtām pṛthām sāntvitām keśavena tadā nā āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam mantriṇam vāsudevam tathā bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam ca teṣām bhāradvājam ca āśiṣaḥ anubruvāṇam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam karṇaḥ uvāca bhīṣmam na aham yotsye yudhyamāne tvayi iti hitvā senām apacakrāma ca eva tadā nā āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vāsudeva arjunau tau tathā dhanuḥ gāṇḍivam aprameyam trīṇi ugra vīryāṇi samāgatāni tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya kṛṣṇam lokān darśayānam śarīre yadā aśrauṣam bhīṣmam amitra karśanam nighnantam ājau ayutam rathānām na eṣām kaḥ cit vadhyate dṛśya rūpaḥ tadā nā āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam bhīṣmam atyanta śūram hatam pārthena āhaveṣu apradhṛṣyam śikhaṇḍinam puratas sthāpayitvā tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam śara talpe śayānam vṛddham vīram sāditam citra puṅkhaiḥ bhīṣmam kṛtvā somakān alpa śeṣān tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam śāṃtanave śayāne pānīya arthe ca uditena arjunena bhūmim bhittvā tarpitam tatra bhīṣmam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam śukra sūryau ca yuktau kaunteyānām anulomau jayāya nityam ca asmān śvāpadāḥ vyābhaṣantaḥ tadā nā āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya na pāṇḍavān śreṣṭhatamān nihanti tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam ca asmadīyān mahā rathān vyavasthitān arjunasya antakāya saṃśaptakān nihatān arjunena tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vyūham abhedyam anyaiḥ bhāradvājena ātta śastreṇa guptam bhittvā saubhadram vīram ekam praviṣṭam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā abhimanyum parivārya bālam sarve hatvā hṛṣṭa rūpāḥ babhūvuḥ mahā rathāḥ pārtham a śaknuvantaḥ tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam abhimanyum nihatya harṣāt mūḍhān krośataḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān krodham muktam saindhave ca arjunena yadā aśrauṣam saindhava arthe pratijñām pratijñātām tad vadhāya arjunena satyām nistīrṇām śatru madhye ca tena yadā aśrauṣam śrānta haye dhanaṃjaye muktvā hayān pāyayitvā upavṛttān punar yuktvā vāsudevam prayātam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vāhaneṣu āśvasatsu rathopasthe tiṣṭhatā gāṇḍivena sarvān yodhān vāritān arjunena tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam nāga balaiḥ durutsaham droṇa anīkam yuyudhānam pramathya yātam vārṣṇeyam yatra tau kṛṣṇa pārthau tadā nā āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam karṇam āsādya muktam vadhāt bhīmam kutsayitvā vacobhiḥ dhanuṣkoṭyā tudya karṇena vīram tadā nā āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā droṇaḥ kṛtavarmā kṛpaḥ ca karṇaḥ drauṇiḥ madra rājaḥ ca śūraḥ amarṣayan saindhavam vadhyamānam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam devarājena dattām divyām śaktim vyaṃsitām mādhavena ghaṭotkace rākṣase ghora rūpe tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam karṇa ghaṭotkacābhyām yuddhe muktām sūtaputreṇa śaktim yayā vadhyaḥ samare savyasācī yadā aśrauṣam droṇam ācāryam ekam dhṛṣṭadyumnena abhyatikramya dharmam rathopasthe prāya gatam viśastam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam drauṇinā dvairatha stham mādrī putram nakulam loka madhye samam yuddhe pāṇḍavam yudhyamānam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya na eṣām antam gatavān pāṇḍavānām tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam karṇam atyanta śūram hatam pārthena āhaveṣu apradhṛṣyam tasmin bhrātṝṇām vigrahe deva guhye tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam droṇaputram kṛpam ca duḥśāsanam kṛtavarmāṇam ugram yudhiṣṭhiram śūnyam a dharṣayantam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam nihatam madra rājam raṇe śūram dharmarājena sūta sadā saṃgrāme spardhate yaḥ sa kṛṣṇam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam kalaha dyūta mūlam māyā balam saubalam pāṇḍavena hatam saṃgrāme sahadevena pāpam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam śrāntam ekam śayānam hradam gatvā stambhayitvā tat ambhaḥ duryodhanam viratham bhagna darpam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam pāṇḍavān tiṣṭhamānān gaṅgāhrade vāsudevena sārdham amarṣaṇam dharṣayataḥ sutam me tadā nā āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam vividhān tāta mārgān gadā yuddhe maṇḍalam saṃcarantam mithyā hatam vāsudevasya buddhyā tadā nā āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam droṇaputra ādibhiḥ taiḥ hatān pāñcālān draupadeyān ca suptān kṛtam bībhatsam ayaśasyam ca karma tadā nā āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam bhīmasena anuyātena aśvatthāmnā parama astram prayuktam kruddhena aiṣīkam avadhīt yena garbham tadā nā āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam brahmaśiraḥ arjunena muktam svasti iti astram astreṇa śāntam aśvatthāmnā maṇi ratnam ca dattam tadā na āśaṃse vijayāya saṃjaya yadā aśrauṣam droṇaputreṇa garbhe vairāṭyāḥ vai pātyamāne mahā astre dvaipāyanaḥ keśavaḥ droṇaputram paraspareṇa abhiśāpaiḥ śaśāpa śocyā gāndhārī putra pautraiḥ vihīnā tathā vadhvaḥ pitṛbhiḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ ca kṛtam kāryam duṣkaram pāṇḍaveyaiḥ prāptam rājyam asapatnam punar taiḥ kaṣṭam yuddhe daśa śeṣāḥ śrutāḥ me trayaḥ asmākam pāṇḍavānām ca sapta dvi ūnāḥ viṃśatiḥ āhata akṣauhiṇīnām tasmin saṃgrāme vigrahe kṣatriyāṇām tamasā tu abhyavastīrṇaḥ mohaḥ āviśati iva mām saṃjñām nā upalabhe sūta manaḥ vihvalati iva me iti uktvā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ atha vilapya bahu duḥkhitaḥ mūrcchitaḥ punar āśvastaḥ saṃjayam vākyam abravīt saṃjaya evaṃgate prāṇān tyaktum icchāmi māciram stokam hi api na paśyāmi phalam jīvita dhāraṇe tam tathāvādinam dīnam vilapantam mahīpatim gāvalgaṇiḥ idam dhīmān mahā artham vākyam abravīt śrutavān asi vai rājñaḥ mahā utsāhān mahā balān mahatsu rāja vaṃśeṣu guṇaiḥ samuditeṣu ca jātān divya astra viduṣaḥ śakra pratima tejasaḥ dharmeṇa pṛthivīm jitvā yajñaiḥ iṣṭvā āpta dakṣiṇaiḥ asmin loke yaśaḥ prāpya tatas kāla vaśam gatāḥ vainyam mahā ratham vīram sṛñjayam jayatām varam vāhlīkam damanam śaibyam śaryātim ajitam jitam viśvāmitram amitra ghnam ambarīṣam mahā balam rāmam dāśarathim ca eva śaśabindum bhagīratham yayātim śubha karmāṇam devaiḥ yaḥ yājitaḥ svayam caitya yūpa aṅkitā bhūmiḥ yasya iyam savana ākarā iti rājñām caturviṃśat nāradena sura ṛṣiṇā putra śoka abhitaptāya purā śaibyāya kīrtitāḥ tebhyaḥ ca anye gatāḥ pūrvam rājānaḥ balavattarāḥ mahā rathāḥ mahātmānaḥ sarvaiḥ samuditāḥ guṇaiḥ pūruḥ kuruḥ yaduḥ śūraḥ viṣvagaśvaḥ mahādhṛtiḥ anenāḥ yuvanāśvaḥ ca kakutsthaḥ vikramī raghuḥ vijitī vītihotraḥ ca bhavaḥ śvetaḥ bṛhadguruḥ uśīnaraḥ śatarathaḥ kaṅkaḥ duliduhaḥ drumaḥ ajeyaḥ paraśuḥ puṇḍraḥ śambhuḥ devāvṛdhaḥ anaghaḥ devāhvayaḥ supratimaḥ supratīkaḥ bṛhat rathaḥ mahā utsāhaḥ vinīta ātmā sukratuḥ naiṣadhaḥ nalaḥ satyavrataḥ śāntabhayaḥ sumitraḥ subalaḥ prabhuḥ jānujaṅghaḥ anaraṇyaḥ arkaḥ priya bhṛtyaḥ śubha vrataḥ balabandhuḥ nirāmardaḥ ketuśṛṅgaḥ bṛhat balaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ bṛhatketuḥ dīptaketuḥ nirāmayaḥ avikṣit prabalaḥ dhūrtaḥ kṛtabandhuḥ dṛḍheṣudhiḥ mahā purāṇaḥ saṃbhāvyaḥ pratyaṅgaḥ para hā śrutiḥ ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas śrūyante ayutaśas ca anye saṃkhyātāḥ ca api padmaśas hitvā su vipulān bhogān buddhimantaḥ mahā balāḥ rājānaḥ nidhanam prāptāḥ tava putraiḥ mahattamāḥ yeṣām divyāni karmāṇi vikramaḥ tyāgaḥ eva ca māhātmyam api ca āstikyam satyatā śaucam ārjavam sarva ṛddhi guṇa saṃpannāḥ te ca api nidhanam gatāḥ tava putrāḥ durātmānaḥ prataptāḥ ca eva manyunā lubdhāḥ durvṛtta bhūyiṣṭhāḥ na tān śocitum arhasi śrutavān asi medhāvī buddhimān prājña saṃmataḥ yeṣām śāstra anugā buddhiḥ na te muhyanti bhārata na atyantam eva anuvṛttiḥ śrūyate putra rakṣaṇe daivam prajñā viśeṣeṇa kaḥ nivartitum arhati vidhātṛ vihitam mārgam na kaḥ cit ativartate kāla mūlam idam sarvam bhāva abhāvau sukha asukhe kālaḥ pacati bhūtāni kālaḥ saṃharati prajāḥ nirdahantam prajāḥ kālam kālaḥ śamayate punar kālaḥ vikurute bhāvān sarvān loke śubha aśubhān kālaḥ saṃkṣipate sarvāḥ prajāḥ visṛjate punar kālaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu carati a vidhṛtaḥ samaḥ atīta anāgatāḥ bhāvāḥ ye ca vartanti sāṃpratam tān kāla nirmitān buddhvā na saṃjñām hātum arhasi sūtaḥ uvāca atra upaniṣadam puṇyām kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ abravīt bhārata adhyayanāt puṇyāt api pādam adhīyataḥ śraddadhānasya pūyante sarva pāpāni aśeṣatas kīrtyante śubha karmāṇaḥ tathā yakṣa mahā uragāḥ bhagavān vāsudevaḥ ca kīrtyate atra sanātanaḥ śāśvatam brahma paramam dhruvam jyotiḥ sanātanam yasya divyāni karmāṇi kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ saṃtatiḥ ca pravṛttiḥ ca janma mṛtyuḥ punarbhavaḥ adhyātmam śrūyate yat ca pañca bhūta guṇa ātmakam yat tat yati varāḥ yuktāḥ dhyāna yoga bala anvitāḥ śraddadhānaḥ sadā udyuktaḥ satya dharma parāyaṇaḥ āsevan imam adhyāyam naraḥ pāpāt pramucyate anukramaṇim adhyāyam bhāratasya imam āditas āstikaḥ satatam śṛṇvan na kṛcchreṣu avasīdati anukramaṇyā yāvat syāt ahnā rātryā ca saṃcitam navanītam yathā dadhnaḥ dvipadām brāhmaṇaḥ yathā hradānām udadhiḥ śreṣṭhaḥ gauḥ variṣṭhā catuṣpadām yathā etāni variṣṭhāni tathā bhāratam ucyate yaḥ ca enam śrāvayet śrāddhe brāhmaṇān pādam antatas akṣayyam anna pānam tat pitṝn tasya upatiṣṭhati itihāsa purāṇābhyām vedam samupabṛṃhayet kārṣṇam vedam imam vidvān śrāvayitvā artham aśnute bhrūṇahatyā kṛtam ca api pāpam jahyāt na saṃśayaḥ yaḥ imam śuciḥ adhyāyam paṭhet parvaṇi parvaṇi adhītam bhāratam tena kṛtsnam syāt iti me matiḥ yaḥ ca imam śṛṇuyāt nityam ārṣam śraddhā samanvitaḥ sa dīrgham āyuḥ kīrtim ca svargatim ca āpnuyāt naraḥ samāgataiḥ sura ṛṣibhiḥ tulām āropitam purā ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ sūtaḥ uvāca śuśrūṣā yadi vaḥ viprāḥ bruvataḥ ca kathāḥ śubhāḥ tretā dvāparayoḥ saṃdhau rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ asakṛt pārthivam kṣatram jaghāna amarṣa coditaḥ sa sarvam kṣatram utsādya sva vīryeṇa anala dyutiḥ pitṝn saṃtarpayām āsa rudhireṇa iti naḥ śrutam teṣām samīpe yaḥ deśaḥ hradānām rudhira ambhasām tena eva nāmnā tam deśam vācyam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ samantapañcake yuddham kuru pāṇḍava senayoḥ aṣṭādaśa samājagmuḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ yuyutsayā evam nāma abhinirvṛttam tasya deśasya vai dvijāḥ puṇyaḥ ca ramaṇīyaḥ ca sa deśaḥ vaḥ prakīrtitaḥ yathā deśaḥ sa vikhyātaḥ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ akṣauhiṇyāḥ parīmāṇam ratha aśva nara dantinām sūtaḥ uvāca ekaḥ rathaḥ gajaḥ ca ekaḥ narāḥ pañca padātayaḥ pattim tu triguṇām etām āhuḥ senāmukham budhāḥ trayaḥ gulmāḥ gaṇaḥ nāma vāhinī tu gaṇāḥ trayaḥ smṛtāḥ tisraḥ tu vāhinyaḥ pṛtanā iti vicakṣaṇaiḥ anīkinīm daśa guṇām prāhuḥ akṣauhiṇīm budhāḥ akṣauhiṇyāḥ prasaṃkhyānam rathānām dvijasattamāḥ saṃkhyā gaṇita tattva jñaiḥ sahasrāṇi ekaviṃśatiḥ śatāni upari ca eva aṣṭau tathā bhūyas ca saptatiḥ gajānām tu parīmāṇam etat eva atra nirdiśet jñeyam śata sahasram tu sahasrāṇi tathā nava narāṇām api pañcāśat śatāni trīṇi ca anaghāḥ pañca ṣaṣṭi sahasrāṇi tathā aśvānām śatāni ca daśa uttarāṇi ṣaḍ prāhuḥ yathāvat iha saṃkhyayā etām akṣauhiṇīm prāhuḥ saṃkhyā tattva vidaḥ janāḥ yām vaḥ kathitavān asmi vistareṇa dvijottamāḥ etayā saṃkhyayā hi āsan kuru pāṇḍava senayoḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ piṇḍena aṣṭādaśa eva tāḥ kauravān kāraṇam kṛtvā kālena adbhuta karmaṇā ahāni pañca droṇaḥ tu rarakṣa kuru vāhinīm ākhyāsye tatra paulomam ākhyānam ca āditas param abhipannam naraiḥ prājñaiḥ vairāgyam iva mokṣibhiḥ itihāsaḥ pradhāna arthaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarva āgameṣu ayam svara vyañjanayoḥ kṛtsnā loka veda āśrayā iva vāc bhāratasya itihāsasya śrūyatām parva saṃgrahaḥ parva anukramaṇī pūrvam dvitīyam parva saṃgrahaḥ pauṣyam paulomam āstīkam ādi vaṃśa avatāraṇam tatas svayaṃvaram devyāḥ pāñcālyāḥ parva ca ucyate arjunasya vane vāsaḥ subhadrā haraṇam tatas subhadrā haraṇāt ūrdhvam jñeyam haraṇahārikam tatas khāṇḍava dāha ākhyam tatra eva maya darśanam tatas ca argha abhiharaṇam śiśupāla vadhaḥ tatas īśvara arjunayoḥ yuddham parva kairāta saṃjñitam tīrtha yātrā tatas parva kururājasya dhīmataḥ saṃvādaḥ ca tatas parva draupadī satyabhāmayoḥ ghoṣa yātrā tatas parva mṛga svapna bhayam tatas kuṇḍala āharaṇam parva tatas param iha ucyate āraṇeyam tatas parva vairāṭam tad anantaram kīcakānām vadhaḥ parva parva go grahaṇam tatas abhimanyunā ca vairāṭyāḥ parva vaivāhikam smṛtam tatas saṃjaya yāna ākhyam parva jñeyam atas param prajāgaram tatas parva dhṛtarāṣṭrasya cintayā jñeyam vivāda parva atra karṇasya api mahātmanaḥ niryāṇam parva ca tatas kuru pāṇḍava senayoḥ ulūka dūta āgamanam parva āmarṣa vivardhanam bhīṣma abhiṣecanam parva jñeyam adbhuta kāraṇam jambūkhaṇḍa vinirmāṇam parva uktam tad anantaram droṇa abhiṣekaḥ parva uktam saṃśaptaka vadhaḥ tatas tatas droṇa vadhaḥ parva vijñeyam loma harṣaṇam mokṣaḥ nārāyaṇa astrasya parva anantaram ucyate sārasvatam tatas parva tīrtha vaṃśa guṇa anvitam aiṣīkam parva nirdiṣṭam atas ūrdhvam su dāruṇam śrāddha parva tatas jñeyam kurūṇām aurdhvadehikam ābhiṣecanikam parva dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ cārvāka nigrahaḥ parva rakṣasaḥ brahma rūpiṇaḥ pravibhāgaḥ gṛhāṇām ca parva uktam tad anantaram tatas parva parijñeyam ānuśāsanikam param svarga ārohaṇikam parva tatas bhīṣmasya dhīmataḥ tatas aśvamedhikam parva sarva pāpa praṇāśanam anugītā tatas parva jñeyam adhyātma vācakam parva ca āśrama vāsa ākhyam putra darśanam eva ca mahāprasthānikam parva svarga ārohaṇikam tatas harivaṃśaḥ tatas parva purāṇam khila saṃjñitam etat parva śatam pūrṇam vyāsena uktam mahātmanā yathāvat sūtaputreṇa lomaharṣaṇinā punar kathitam naimiṣa araṇye parvāṇi aṣṭādaśa eva tu samāsaḥ bhāratasya ayam tatra uktaḥ parva saṃgrahaḥ paulome bhṛgu vaṃśasya vistāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ āstīke sarva nāgānām garuḍasya ca saṃbhavaḥ yajataḥ sarpa satreṇa rājñaḥ pārikṣitasya ca kathā iyam abhinirvṛttā bhāratānām mahātmanām vividhāḥ saṃbhavāḥ rājñām uktāḥ saṃbhava parvaṇi anyeṣām ca eva viprāṇām ṛṣeḥ dvaipāyanasya ca aṃśāvataraṇam ca atra devānām parikīrtitam daityānām dānavānām ca yakṣāṇām ca mahā ojasām nāgānām atha sarpāṇām gandharvāṇām patatriṇām anyeṣām ca eva bhūtānām vividhānām samudbhavaḥ vasūnām punar utpattiḥ bhāgīrathyām mahātmanām śaṃtanoḥ veśmani punar teṣām ca ārohaṇam divi tejaḥ oṃśānām ca saṃghātāt bhīṣmasya api atra saṃbhavaḥ pratijñā pālanam ca eva rakṣā citrāṅgadasya ca hate citrāṅgade ca eva rakṣā bhrātuḥ yavīyasaḥ dharmasya nṛṣu saṃbhūtiḥ aṇīmāṇḍavya śāpa jā kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāt ca eva prasūtiḥ vara dāna jā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya pāṇḍoḥ ca pāṇḍavānām ca saṃbhavaḥ pāṇḍavānām vane ghore hiḍimbāyāḥ ca darśanam a jñāta caryā pāṇḍūnām vāsaḥ brāhmaṇa veśmani bakasya nidhanam ca eva nāgarāṇām ca vismayaḥ aṅgāraparṇam nirjitya gaṅgā kūle arjunaḥ tadā bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ pāñcālān abhitas yayau tāpatyam atha vāsiṣṭham aurvam ca ākhyānam uttamam pañca indrāṇām upākhyānam atra eva adbhutam ucyate draupadyāḥ deva vihitaḥ vivāhaḥ ca api amānuṣaḥ khāṇḍavaprastha vāsaḥ ca tathā rājya ardha śāsanam nāradasya ājñayā ca eva draupadyāḥ samayakriyā pārthasya vana vāsaḥ ca ulūpyā pathi saṃgamaḥ puṇya tīrtha anusaṃyānam babhruvāhana janma ca dvārakāyām subhadrā ca kāmayānena kāminī vāsudevasya anumate prāptā ca eva kirīṭinā haraṇam gṛhya saṃprāpte kṛṣṇe devakī nandane saṃprāptiḥ cakra dhanuṣoḥ khāṇḍavasya ca dāhanam mahā ṛṣeḥ mandapālasya śārṅgyam tanaya saṃbhavaḥ adhyāyānām śate dve tu saṃkhyāte parama ṛṣiṇā aṣṭādaśa eva ca adhyāyāḥ vyāsena uttama tejasā sapta śloka sahasrāṇi tathā nava śatāni ca ślokāḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ granthaḥ mahātmanā sabhā kriyā pāṇḍavānām kiṃkarāṇām ca darśanam lokapāla sabhā ākhyānam nāradāt devadarśanāt rājasūyasya ca ārambhaḥ jarāsaṃdha vadhaḥ tathā girivraje niruddhānām rājñām kṛṣṇena mokṣaṇam rājasūye argha saṃvāde śiśupāla vadhaḥ tathā yajñe vibhūtim tām dṛṣṭvā duḥkha amarṣa anvitasya ca yatra dyūta arṇave magnān draupadī nauḥ iva arṇavāt tārayām āsa tān tīrṇān jñātvā duryodhanaḥ nṛpaḥ punar eva tatas dyūte samāhvayata pāṇḍavān etat sarvam sabhāparva samākhyātam mahātmanā adhyāyāḥ saptatiḥ jñeyāḥ tathā dvau ca atra saṃkhyayā ślokānām dve sahasre tu pañca śloka śatāni ca ślokāḥ ca ekādaśa jñeyāḥ parvaṇi asmin prakīrtitāḥ atas param tṛtīyam tu jñeyam āraṇyakam mahat vṛṣṇīnām āgamaḥ yatra pāñcālānām ca sarvaśas darśanam lokapālānām svarga ārohaṇam eva ca darśanam bṛhadaśvasya mahā ṛṣeḥ bhāvitātmanaḥ vana vāsa gatānām ca pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām tīrtha yātrā tathā eva atra pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām yatra mandāra puṣpa artham nalinīm tām adharṣayat yakṣaiḥ ca api mahā vīryaiḥ maṇimat pramukhaiḥ tathā āgastyam api ca ākhyānam yatra vātāpi bhakṣaṇam indraḥ agniḥ yatra dharmaḥ ca ajijñāsan śibim nṛpam ṛśyaśṛṅgasya caritam kaumārabrahmacāriṇaḥ kārtavīrya vadhaḥ yatra haihayānām ca varṇyate śaryāti yajñe nāsatyau kṛtavān soma pīthinau putra artham ayajat rājā lebhe putra śatam ca saḥ vijitya sāgaram prāptam pitaram labdhavān ṛṣiḥ avāpya divyāni astrāṇi guru arthe savyasācinā ghoṣa yātrā ca gandharvaiḥ yatra yuddham kirīṭinaḥ punarāgamanam ca eva teṣām dvaitavanam saraḥ jayadrathena apahāraḥ draupadyāḥ ca āśrama antarāt mārkaṇḍeya samasyāyām upākhyānāni bhāgaśas saṃdarśanam ca kṛṣṇasya saṃvādaḥ ca eva satyayā karṇasya parimoṣaḥ atra kuṇḍalābhyām puraṃdarāt āraṇeyam upākhyānam yatra dharmaḥ anvaśāt sutam jagmuḥ labdha varāḥ yatra pāṇḍavāḥ paścimām diśam etat āraṇyakam parva tṛtīyam parikīrtitam atra adhyāya śate dve tu saṃkhyāte parama ṛṣiṇā ekonasaptatiḥ ca eva tathā adhyāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ekādaśa sahasrāṇi ślokānām ṣaṣ śatāni ca catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ tathā ślokāḥ parva etat parikīrtitam atas param nibodha idam vairāṭam parva vistaram virāṭa nagaram gatvā śmaśāne vipulām śamīm dṛṣṭvā saṃnidadhuḥ tatra pāṇḍavāḥ āyudhāni uta go dhanam ca virāṭasya mokṣitam yatra pāṇḍavaiḥ virāṭena uttarā dattā snuṣā yatra kirīṭinaḥ atra api parisaṃkhyātam adhyāyānām mahātmanā saptaṣaṣṭiḥ atho pūrṇā śloka agram api me śṛṇu ślokānām dve sahasre tu ślokāḥ pañcāśat eva tu parvaṇi asmin samākhyātāḥ saṃkhyayā parama ṛṣiṇā udyogaparva vijñeyam pañcamam śṛṇu atas param upaplavye niviṣṭeṣu pāṇḍaveṣu jigīṣayā iti ukte vacane kṛṣṇaḥ yatra uvāca mahāmatiḥ ayudhyamānam ātmānam mantriṇam puruṣa ṛṣabhau akṣauhiṇīm vā sainyasya kasya vā kim dadāmi aham ayudhyamānam sacivam vavre kṛṣṇam dhanaṃjayaḥ saṃjayam preṣayām āsa śama artham pāṇḍavān prati yatra dūtam mahā rājaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ pratāpavān śrutvā ca pāṇḍavān yatra vāsudeva purogamān prajāgaraḥ saṃprajajñe dhṛtarāṣṭrasya cintayā śrāvayām āsa rājānam dhṛtarāṣṭram manīṣiṇam manaḥ tāpa anvitaḥ rājā śrāvitaḥ śoka lālasaḥ yatra kṛṣṇaḥ dayā āpannaḥ saṃdhim icchan mahā yaśāḥ svayam āgāt śamam kartum nagaram nāgasāhvayam pratyākhyānam ca kṛṣṇasya rājñā duryodhanena vai śama artham yācamānasya pakṣayoḥ ubhayoḥ hitam karṇa duryodhana ādīnām duṣṭam vijñāya mantritam yoga īśvara tvam kṛṣṇena yatra rājasu darśitam ratham āropya kṛṣṇena yatra karṇaḥ anumantritaḥ upāya pūrvam śauṇḍīryāt pratyākhyātaḥ ca tena saḥ tatas ca api abhiniryātrā ratha aśva nara dantinām yatra rājñā ulūkasya preṣaṇam pāṇḍavān prati śvas bhāvini mahā yuddhe dūtyena krūra vādinā etat su bahu vṛttāntam pañcamam parva bhārate adhyāyāḥ saṃkhyayā tu atra ṣaḍaśīti śatam smṛtam ślokānām ṣaḍ sahasrāṇi tāvanti eva śatāni ca ślokāḥ ca navatiḥ proktāḥ tathā eva aṣṭau mahātmanā vyāsena udāra matinā parvaṇi asmin tapodhanāḥ atas ūrdhvam vicitra artham bhīṣmaparva pracakṣate jambūkhaṇḍa vinirmāṇam yatra uktam saṃjayena ha yatra yuddham abhūt ghoram daśa ahāni ati dāruṇam kaśmalam yatra pārthasya vāsudevaḥ mahāmatiḥ moha jam nāśayām āsa hetubhiḥ mokṣa darśanaiḥ śikhaṇḍinam puraskṛtya yatra pārthaḥ mahā dhanuḥ vinighnan niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ rathāt bhīṣmam apātayat ṣaṣṭham etat mahā parva bhārate parikīrtitam adhyāyānām śatam proktam saptadaśa tathā apare pañca śloka sahasrāṇi saṃkhyayā aṣṭau śatāni ca ślokāḥ ca parvaṇi asmin prakīrtitāḥ vyāsena veda viduṣā saṃkhyātāḥ bhīṣmaparvaṇi yatra saṃśaptakāḥ pārtham apaninyuḥ raṇa ajirāt supratīkena nāgena saha śastaḥ kirīṭinā jayadratha mukhāḥ bālam śūram aprāpta yauvanam akṣauhiṇīḥ sapta hatvā hataḥ rājā jayadrathaḥ saṃśaptaka avaśeṣam ca kṛtam niḥśeṣam āhave alambusaḥ śrutāyuḥ ca jalasaṃdhaḥ ca vīryavān saumadattiḥ virāṭaḥ ca drupadaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ ghaṭotkaca ādayaḥ ca anye nihatāḥ droṇaparvaṇi aśvatthāmā api ca atrā eva droṇe yudhi nipātite astram prāduścakāra ugram nārāyaṇam amarṣitaḥ atra te pṛthivī pālāḥ prāyaśas nidhanam gatāḥ droṇaparvaṇi ye śūrāḥ nirdiṣṭāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ adhyāyānām śatam proktam adhyāyāḥ saptatiḥ tathā aṣṭau śloka sahasrāṇi tathā nava śatāni ca ślokāḥ nava tathā eva atra saṃkhyātāḥ tattva darśinā pārāśaryeṇa muninā saṃcintya droṇaparvaṇi ākhyātam yatra paurāṇam tripurasya nipātanam prayāṇe paruṣaḥ ca atra saṃvādaḥ karṇa śalyayoḥ haṃsakākīyam ākhyānam atra eva ākṣepa saṃhitam aṣṭamam parva nirdiṣṭam etat bhārata cintakaiḥ ekonasaptatiḥ proktāḥ adhyāyāḥ karṇaparvaṇi catvāri eva sahasrāṇi nava śloka śatāni ca vṛttāni ratha yuddhāni kīrtyante yatra bhāgaśas vināśaḥ kuru mukhyānām śalyaparvaṇi kīrtyate śalyasya nidhanam ca atra dharmarājāt mahā rathāt sarasvatyāḥ ca tīrthānām puṇya tā parikīrtitā ekonaṣaṣṭiḥ adhyāyāḥ tatra saṃkhyā viśāradaiḥ saṃkhyātāḥ bahu vṛttāntāḥ śloka agram ca atra śasyate trīṇi śloka sahasrāṇi dve śate viṃśatiḥ tathā muninā saṃpraṇītāni kauravāṇām yaśaḥ bhṛtām atas param pravakṣyāmi sauptikam parva dāruṇam vyapayāteṣu pārtheṣu trayaḥ te abhyāyayuḥ rathāḥ kṛtavarmā kṛpaḥ drauṇiḥ sāyāhne rudhira ukṣitāḥ a hatvā sarva pāñcālān dhṛṣṭadyumna purogamān pāṇḍavān ca sahāmātyān na vimokṣyāmi daṃśanam prasuptān niśi viśvastān yatra te puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ pāñcālān sa parīvārān jaghnuḥ drauṇi purogamāḥ yatra amucyanta pārthāḥ te pañca kṛṣṇa bala āśrayāt sātyakiḥ ca mahā iṣvāsaḥ śeṣāḥ ca nidhanam gatāḥ draupadī putra śoka ārtā pitṛ bhrātṛ vadha arditā kṛta anaśana saṃkalpā yatra bhartṝn upāviśat draupadī vacanāt yatra bhīmaḥ bhīma parākramaḥ a pāṇḍavāya iti ruṣā drauṇiḥ astram avāsṛjat mā evam iti abravīt kṛṣṇaḥ śamayan tasya tat vacaḥ drauṇi dvaipāyana ādīnām śāpāḥ ca anyonya kāritāḥ toyakarmaṇi sarveṣām rājñām udakadānike gūḍha utpannasya ca ākhyānam karṇasya pṛthayā ātmanaḥ aṣṭādaśā asmin adhyāyāḥ parvaṇi uktāḥ mahātmanā śloka agram atra kathitam śatāni aṣṭau tathā eva ca ślokāḥ ca saptatiḥ proktāḥ yathāvat abhisaṃkhyayā atas ūrdhvam idam prāhuḥ strīparva karuṇā udayam vilāpaḥ vīra patnīnām yatra ati karuṇaḥ smṛtaḥ krodha āveśaḥ prasādaḥ ca gāndhārī dhṛtarāṣṭrayoḥ yatra tān kṣatriyān śūrān diṣṭāntān anivartinaḥ putrān bhrātṝn pitṝn ca eva dadṛśuḥ nihatān raṇe yatra rājā mahā prājñaḥ sarva dharma bhṛtām varaḥ rājñām tāni śarīrāṇi dāhayām āsa śāstrataḥ etat ekādaśam proktam parva ati karuṇam mahat saptaviṃśatiḥ adhyāyāḥ parvaṇi asmin udāhṛtāḥ ślokāḥ saptaśatam ca atra pañcasaptatiḥ ucyate saṃkhyayā bhārata ākhyānam kartrā hi atra mahātmanā atas param śāntiparva dvādaśam buddhi vardhanam ghātayitvā pitṝn bhrātṝn putrān saṃbandhi bāndhavān śāntiparvaṇi dharmāḥ ca vyākhyātāḥ śaratalpikāḥ āpad dharmāḥ ca tatra eva kāla hetu pradarśakāḥ yān buddhvā puruṣaḥ samyak sarvajña tvam avāpnuyāt mokṣa dharmāḥ ca kathitāḥ vicitrāḥ bahu vistarāḥ dvādaśam parva nirdiṣṭam etat prājña jana priyam parvaṇi atra parijñeyam adhyāyānām śata trayam triṃśat ca eva tathā adhyāyāḥ nava ca eva tapodhanāḥ ślokānām tu sahasrāṇi kīrtitāni caturdaśa pañca ca eva śatāni āhuḥ pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyayā atas ūrdhvam tu vijñeyam uttamam bhīṣmāt bhāgīrathī putrāt kururājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vividhānām ca dānānām phala yogāḥ pṛthagvidhāḥ tathā pātra viśeṣāḥ ca dānānām ca paraḥ vidhiḥ etat su bahu vṛttāntam uttamam ca anuśāsanam bhīṣmasya atrā eva saṃprāptiḥ svargasya parikīrtitā adhyāyānām śatam ca atra ṣaṭcatvāriṃśat eva ca ślokānām tu sahasrāṇi ṣaṣ sapta eva śatāni ca suvarṇa kośa saṃprāptiḥ janma ca uktam parikṣitaḥ dagdhasya astra agninā pūrvam kṛṣṇāt saṃjīvanam punar caryāyām hayam utsṛṣṭam pāṇḍavasya anugacchataḥ citrāṅgadāyāḥ putreṇa putrikāyāḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ saṃgrāme babhruvāhena saṃśayam ca atra darśitaḥ atra adhyāya śatam triṃśat trayaḥ adhyāyāḥ ca śabditāḥ trīṇi śloka sahasrāṇi tāvanti eva śatāni ca viṃśatiḥ ca tathā ślokāḥ saṃkhyātāḥ tattva darśinā tatas parva pañcadaśam smṛtam yatra rājyam parityajya gāndhārī sahitaḥ nṛpaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra āśrama padam viduraḥ ca jagāma ha yam dṛṣṭvā prasthitam sādhvī pṛthā api anuyayau tadā putra rājyam parityajya guru śuśrūṣaṇe ratā yatra rājā hatān putrān pautrān anyān ca pārthivān loka antara gatān vīrān apaśyat punar āgatān ṛṣeḥ prasādāt kṛṣṇasya dṛṣṭvā āścaryam anuttamam tyaktvā śokam sa dāraḥ ca siddhim paramikām gataḥ saṃjayaḥ ca mahāmātraḥ vidvān gāvalgaṇiḥ vaśī dadarśa nāradam yatra dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ nāradāt ca eva śuśrāva vṛṣṇīnām kadanam mahat etat āśrama vāsa ākhyam pūrva uktam su mahā adbhutam dvicatvāriṃśat adhyāyāḥ parva etat abhisaṃkhyayā sahasram ekam ślokānām pañca śloka śatāni ca ṣaṭ eva ca tathā ślokāḥ saṃkhyātāḥ tattva darśinā atas param nibodha idam mausalam parva dāruṇam yatra te puruṣa vyāghrāḥ śastra sparśa sahāḥ yudhi brahmadaṇḍa viniṣpiṣṭāḥ samīpe lavaṇa ambhasaḥ āpāne pāna galitāḥ daivena abhipracoditāḥ yatra sarva kṣayam kṛtvā tau ubhau rāma keśavau na aticakramatuḥ kālam prāptam sarva haram samam yatra arjunaḥ dvāravatīm etya vṛṣṇi vinākṛtām dṛṣṭvā viṣādam agamat parām ca ārtim nara ṛṣabhaḥ sa satkṛtya yaduśreṣṭham mātulam śaurim ātmanaḥ dadarśa yadu vīrāṇām āpāne vaiśasam mahat śarīram vāsudevasya rāmasya ca mahātmanaḥ saṃskāram lambhayām āsa vṛṣṇīnām ca pradhānataḥ sa vṛddha bālam ādāya dvāravatyāḥ tatas janam dadarśa āpadi kaṣṭāyām gāṇḍīvasya parābhavam sarveṣām ca eva divyānām astrāṇām a prasanna tām nāśam vṛṣṇi kalatrāṇām prabhāvānām anitya tām dṛṣṭvā nirvedam āpannaḥ vyāsa vākya pracoditaḥ dharmarājam samāsādya saṃnyāsam samarocayet iti etat mausalam parva ṣoḍaśam parikīrtitam adhyāya aṣṭau samākhyātāḥ ślokānām ca śata trayam mahāprasthānikam tasmāt ūrdhvam saptadaśam smṛtam yatra rājyam parityajya pāṇḍavāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ draupadyā sahitāḥ devyā siddhim paramikām gatāḥ atra adhyāyāḥ trayaḥ proktāḥ ślokānām ca śatam tathā viṃśatiḥ ca tathā ślokāḥ saṃkhyātāḥ tattva darśinā adhyāyāḥ pañca saṃkhyātāḥ parva etat abhisaṃkhyayā ślokānām dve śate ca eva prasaṃkhyāte tapodhanāḥ aṣṭādaśa evam etāni parvāṇi uktāni aśeṣatas etat akhilam ākhyātam bhāratam parva saṃgrahāt aṣṭādaśa samājagmuḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ yuyutsayā tat mahat dāruṇam yuddham ahāni aṣṭādaśa abhavat yaḥ vidyāt caturaḥ vedān sāṅga upaniṣadān dvijaḥ na ca ākhyānam idam vidyāt na eva sa syāt vicakṣaṇaḥ śrutvā tu idam upākhyānam śrāvyam anyat na rocate puṃskokila rutam śrutvā rūkṣā dhvāṅkṣasya vāc iva asya ākhyānasya viṣaye purāṇam vartate dvijāḥ kriyā guṇānām sarveṣām idam ākhyānam āśrayaḥ indriyāṇām samastānām citrāḥ iva manaḥ kriyāḥ an āśritya etat ākhyānam kathā bhuvi na vidyate āhāram an apāśritya śarīrasya iva dhāraṇam dvaipāyana oṣṭha puṭa niḥsṛtam aprameyam puṇyam pavitram atha pāpa haram śivam ca śrutvā ādau bhavati nṛṇām sukha avagāham vistīrṇam lavaṇa jalam yathā plavena sūtaḥ uvāca janamejayaḥ pārikṣitaḥ saha bhrātṛbhiḥ kurukṣetre dīrgha satram upāste teṣu tat satram upāsīneṣu tatra śvā abhyāgacchat sārameyaḥ tam mātā rorūyamāṇam uvāca kim rodiṣi tam mātā pratyuvāca sa tām punar uvāca na aparādhyāmi kim cit na avekṣe havīṃṣi na avalihe iti yasmāt ca ayam abhihataḥ anapakārī tasmāt adṛṣṭam tvām bhayam āgamiṣyati iti sa janamejayaḥ evam uktaḥ devaśunyā saramayā dṛḍham saṃbhrāntaḥ viṣaṇṇaḥ ca āsīt sa kadā cit mṛgayām yātaḥ pārikṣitaḥ janamejayaḥ kasmin cit sva viṣaya uddeśe āśramam apaśyat tatra kaḥ cit ṛṣiḥ āsām cakre śrutaśravāḥ nāma tasya abhimataḥ putraḥ āste somaśravāḥ nāma sa namaskṛtya tam ṛṣim uvāca mahā tapasvī svādhyāya saṃpannaḥ mad tapaḥ vīrya saṃbhṛtaḥ mad śukram pītavatyāḥ tasyāḥ kukṣau saṃvṛddhaḥ samarthaḥ ayam bhavataḥ sarvāḥ pāpa kṛtyāḥ śamayitum antareṇa mahādeva kṛtyām bhagavan tathā bhaviṣyati iti sa tam purohitam upādāya upāvṛttaḥ bhrātṝn uvāca mayā ayam vṛtaḥ upādhyāyaḥ sa tathā bhrātṝn saṃdiśya takṣaśilām pratyabhipratasthe tam ca deśam vaśe sthāpayām āsa etasmin antare kaḥ cit ṛṣiḥ dhaumyaḥ nāma āyodaḥ saḥ ekam śiṣyam āruṇim pāñcālyam preṣayām āsa gaccha kedārakhaṇḍam badhāna iti sa upādhyāyena saṃdiṣṭaḥ āruṇiḥ pāñcālyaḥ tatra gatvā tat kedārakhaṇḍam baddhum na aśaknot sa kliśyamānaḥ apaśyat upāyam bhavatu evam kariṣyāmi iti sa tatra saṃviveśa kedārakhaṇḍe tatas kadā cit upādhyāyaḥ āyodaḥ dhaumyaḥ śiṣyān apṛcchat kva āruṇiḥ pāñcālyaḥ gataḥ iti te pratyūcuḥ saḥ evam uktaḥ tān śiṣyān pratyuvāca sa tatra gatvā tasya āhvānāya śabdam cakāra bho āruṇe pāñcālya kva asi sa tat śrutvā āruṇiḥ upādhyāya vākyam tasmāt kedārakhaṇḍāt sahasā utthāya tam upādhyāyam upatasthe ayam asmi atra kedārakhaṇḍe niḥsaramāṇam udakam avāraṇīyam saṃroddhum saṃviṣṭaḥ bhagavat śabdam śrutvā eva sahasā vidārya kedārakhaṇḍam bhavantam upasthitaḥ ājñāpayatu bhavān kim karavāṇi iti tam upādhyāyaḥ abravīt yasmāt bhavān kedārakhaṇḍam avadārya utthitaḥ tasmāt bhavān uddālakaḥ eva nāmnā bhaviṣyati iti saḥ upādhyāyena anugṛhītaḥ yasmāt tvayā mad vacaḥ anuṣṭhitam tasmāt śreyaḥ avāpsyasi iti sarve ca te vedāḥ pratibhāsyanti sarvāṇi ca dharmaśāstrāṇi iti saḥ evam uktaḥ upādhyāyena iṣṭam deśam jagāma tam upādhyāyaḥ preṣayām āsa saḥ upādhyāya vacanāt arakṣat gāḥ sa ca ahani gāḥ rakṣitvā divasa kṣaye abhyāgamya upādhyāyasya agratas sthitvā namaścakre tam upādhyāyaḥ pīvānam apaśyat pīvān asi dṛḍham iti saḥ upādhyāyam pratyuvāca bhaikṣeṇa vṛttim kalpayāmi iti tam upādhyāyaḥ pratyuvāca rakṣitvā ca āgamya tathā eva upādhyāyasya agratas sthitvā namaścakre tam upādhyāyaḥ tathā api pīvānam eva dṛṣṭvā uvāca vatsa upamanyo sarvam aśeṣatas te bhaikṣam gṛhṇāmi kena idānīm vṛttim kalpayasi iti tena vṛttim kalpayāmi iti tam upādhyāyaḥ pratyuvāca na eṣā nyāyyā guru vṛttiḥ anyeṣām api vṛtti uparodham karoṣi evam vartamānaḥ rakṣitvā ca punar upādhyāya gṛham āgamya upādhyāyasya agratas sthitvā namaścakre tam upādhyāyaḥ tathā api pīvānam eva dṛṣṭvā punar uvāca aham te sarvam bhaikṣam gṛhṇāmi na ca anyat carasi pīvān asi saḥ upādhyāyam pratyuvāca bho etāsām gavām payasā vṛttim kalpayāmi iti tam upādhyāyaḥ pratyuvāca tam upādhyāyaḥ pīvānam eva apaśyat bhaikṣam na aśnāsi na ca anyat carasi pīvān asi bhoḥ phenam pibāmi yam ime vatsāḥ mātṝṇām stanam pibantaḥ udgiranti iti tam upādhyāyaḥ pratyuvāca tat evam api vatsānām vṛtti uparodham karoṣi evam vartamānaḥ sa tathā iti pratijñāya nirāhāraḥ tāḥ gāḥ arakṣat tathā pratiṣiddhaḥ bhaikṣam na aśnāti na ca anyat carati sa kadā cit araṇye kṣudhā ārtaḥ arka patrāṇi abhakṣayat sa taiḥ arka patraiḥ bhakṣitaiḥ kṣāra kaṭu uṣṇa vipākibhiḥ cakṣuṣi upahataḥ andhaḥ abhavat saḥ andhaḥ api caṅkramyamāṇaḥ kūpe apatat atha tasmin an āgacchati upādhyāyaḥ śiṣyān avocat sa tad āhvānam upādhyāyāt śrutvā pratyuvāca uccais tam upādhyāyaḥ pratyuvāca arka patrāṇi bhakṣayitvā andhībhūtaḥ asmi tam upādhyāyaḥ pratyuvāca tau tvām cakṣuṣmantam kariṣyataḥ devabhiṣajau iti pra pūrva gau pūrva jau citra bhānū tāvat su vṛttau anamanta māyayā sattamāḥ gāḥ aruṇāḥ udāvahan ṣaṣṭiḥ ca gāvaḥ tri śatāḥ ca dhenavaḥ ekam vatsam suvate tam duhanti nānā goṣṭhāḥ vihitāḥ eka dohanāḥ tau aśvinau duhataḥ gharmam ukthyam ekām nābhim sapta śatāḥ arāḥ śritāḥ pradhiṣu anyāḥ viṃśatiḥ arpitāḥ arāḥ a nemi cakram parivartate ajaram māyā aśvinau samanakti carṣaṇī ekam cakram vartate dvādaśa aram pradhi ṣaṇṇābhim eka akṣam amṛtasya dhāraṇam yasmin devāḥ adhi viśve viṣaktāḥ tau aśvinau muñcataḥ mā viṣīdatam aśvinau indram amṛtam vṛtta bhūyau tirodhattām aśvinau dāsa patnī yuvām diśaḥ janayathaḥ daśa agre samānam mūrdhni rathayāḥ viyanti tāsām yātam ṛṣayaḥ anuprayānti devāḥ manuṣyāḥ kṣitim ācaranti yuvām varṇān vikuruthaḥ viśva rūpān te adhikṣiyanti bhuvanāni viśvā te bhānavaḥ api anusṛtāḥ caranti devāḥ manuṣyāḥ kṣitim ācaranti tau nāsatyau aśvinau āmahe vām srajam ca yām bibhṛthaḥ puṣkarasya tau nāsatyau amṛtau ṛtāvṛdhau ṛte devāḥ tat prapadena sūte evam tena abhiṣṭutau aśvinau ājagmatuḥ āhatuḥ ca enam prītau svaḥ eṣa te apūpaḥ aśāna enam iti tatas tam aśvinau ūcatuḥ āvābhyām purastāt bhavataḥ upādhyāyena evam eva abhiṣṭutābhyām apūpaḥ prītābhyām dattaḥ tam aśvinau āhatuḥ prītau svaḥ tava anayā guru vṛttyā upādhyāyasya te kārṣṇāyasāḥ dantāḥ cakṣuṣmān ca bhaviṣyasi śreyaḥ ca avāpsyasi iti saḥ evam uktaḥ aśvibhyām labdha cakṣuḥ upādhyāya sakāśam āgamya upādhyāyam abhivādya ācacakṣe sa ca asya prītimān abhūt yathā aśvinau āhatuḥ tathā tvam śreyaḥ avāpsyasi iti eṣā tasya api parīkṣā upamanyoḥ tam upādhyāyaḥ saṃdideśa bhavatā mad gṛhe kam cit kālam śuśrūṣamāṇena bhavitavyam śreyaḥ te bhaviṣyati iti sa tathā iti uktvā guru kule dīrgha kālam guru śuśrūṣaṇa paraḥ avasat gauḥ iva nityam guruṣu dhūrṣu niyujyamānaḥ śīta uṣṇa kṣudh tṛṣṇā duḥkha sahaḥ sarvatra a pratikūlaḥ tasya mahatā kālena guruḥ paritoṣam jagāma tad paritoṣāt ca śreyaḥ sarvajña tām ca avāpa eṣā tasya api parīkṣā vedasya saḥ upādhyāyena anujñātaḥ samāvṛttaḥ tasmāt guru kula vāsāt gṛha āśramam pratyapadyata tasya api sva gṛhe vasataḥ trayaḥ śiṣyāḥ babhūvuḥ sa śiṣyān na kim cit uvāca karma vā kriyatām guru śuśrūṣā vā iti duḥkha abhijñaḥ hi guru kula vāsasya śiṣyān parikleśena yojayitum na iyeṣa atha kasya cit kālasya vedam brāhmaṇam janamejayaḥ pauṣyaḥ ca kṣatriyau upetya upādhyāyam varayām cakratuḥ sa kadā cit yājya kāryeṇa abhiprasthitaḥ uttaṅkam nāma śiṣyam niyojayām āsa saḥ evam pratisamādiśya uttaṅkam vedaḥ pravāsam jagāma sa vasan tatra upādhyāya strībhiḥ sahitābhiḥ āhūya uktaḥ upādhyāyinī te ṛtumatī upādhyāyaḥ ca proṣitaḥ etat viṣīdati iti na mayā strīṇām vacanāt idam akāryam kāryam na hi aham upādhyāyena saṃdiṣṭaḥ tasya punar upādhyāyaḥ kāla antareṇa gṛhān upajagāma tasmāt pravāsāt sa tad vṛttam tasya aśeṣam upalabhya prītimān abhūt vatsa uttaṅka kim te priyam karavāṇi iti dharmataḥ hi śuśrūṣitaḥ asmi bhavatā tena prītiḥ paraspareṇa nau saṃvṛddhā kim te priyam karavāṇi iti evam hi āhuḥ yaḥ ca adharmeṇa vibrūyāt yaḥ ca adharmeṇa pṛcchati vatsa uttaṅka uṣyatām tāvat iti sa kadā cit tam upādhyāyam āha uttaṅkaḥ ājñāpayatu bhavān tam upādhyāyaḥ pratyuvāca enām praviśya upādhyāyinīm pṛccha kim upaharāmi iti saḥ evam uktaḥ upādhyāyena upādhyāyinīm apṛcchat bhavati upādhyāyena asmi anujñātaḥ gṛham gantum tat icchāmi iṣṭam te guru artham upahṛtya anṛṇaḥ gantum tat ājñāpayatu bhavatī gaccha pauṣyam rājānam tābhyām ābaddhābhyām brāhmaṇān pariveṣṭum icchāmi śobhamānā yathā tābhyām kuṇḍalābhyām tasmin ahani saṃpādayasva śreyaḥ hi te syāt kṣaṇam kurvate iti saḥ evam uktaḥ upādhyāyinyā prātiṣṭhata uttaṅkaḥ sa pathi gacchan apaśyat ṛṣabham atipramāṇam tam adhirūḍham ca puruṣam atipramāṇam eva tam āha puruṣaḥ bhūyaḥ mā vicāraya upādhyāyena api te bhakṣitam pūrvam iti saḥ evam uktaḥ bāḍham iti uktvā tadā tat ṛṣabhasya purīṣam mūtram ca bhakṣayitvā uttaṅkaḥ pratasthe yatra sa kṣatriyaḥ pauṣyaḥ tam upetya apaśyat uttaṅkaḥ āsīnam kim karavāṇi iti tam uvāca uttaṅkaḥ guru arthe kuṇḍalābhyām arthī āgataḥ asmi iti ye te kṣatriyayā pinaddhe kuṇḍale te bhavān dātum arhati iti tam pauṣyaḥ pratyuvāca praviśya antaḥpuram kṣatriyā yācyatām iti sa tena evam uktaḥ praviśya antaḥpuram kṣatriyām na apaśyat sa pauṣyam punar uvāca na hi te kṣatriyā antaḥpure saṃnihitā na enām paśyāmi iti saṃprati bhavān ucchiṣṭaḥ na hi sā kṣatriyā ucchiṣṭena aśucinā vā śakyā draṣṭum pativratā tvāt eṣā na aśuceḥ darśanam upaiti iti asti khalu mayā ucchiṣṭena upaspṛṣṭam śīghram gacchatā ca iti tam pauṣyaḥ pratyuvāca atha uttaṅkaḥ tathā iti uktvā prāc mukhaḥ upaviśya su prakṣālita pāṇi pāda vadanaḥ aśabdābhiḥ hṛdayaṃgamābhiḥ adbhiḥ upaspṛśya tris pītvā dvis parimṛjya khāni adbhiḥ upaspṛśya antaḥpuram praviśya tām kṣatriyām apaśyat sā ca dṛṣṭvā eva uttaṅkam abhyutthāya abhivādya uvāca ājñāpaya kim karavāṇi iti sa tām uvāca ete kuṇḍale takṣakaḥ nāga rājaḥ prārthayati saḥ evam uktaḥ tām kṣatriyām pratyuvāca na mām śaktaḥ takṣakaḥ nāga rājaḥ dharṣayitum iti saḥ evam uktvā tām kṣatriyām āmantrya pauṣya sakāśam āgacchat sa tam dṛṣṭvā uvāca bhoḥ pauṣya prītaḥ asmi iti tam pauṣyaḥ pratyuvāca bhagavan cirasya pātram āsādyate bhavān ca guṇavān atithiḥ tat kariṣye śrāddham kṣaṇaḥ kriyatām iti kṛtakṣaṇaḥ eva asmi atha uttaṅkaḥ śītam annam sa keśam dṛṣṭvā aśuci etat iti matvā pauṣyam uvāca tam pauṣyaḥ pratyuvāca yasmāt tvam api aduṣṭam annam dūṣayasi tasmāt anapatyaḥ bhaviṣyasi iti saḥ atha pauṣyaḥ tasya aśuci bhāvam annasya āgamayām āsa atha tat annam mukta keśyā striyā upahṛtam sa keśam aśuci matvā uttaṅkam prasādayām āsa bhagavan ajñānāt etat annam sa keśam upahṛtam śītam ca na mṛṣā bravīmi tam pauṣyaḥ pratyuvāca na aham śaktaḥ śāpam pratyādātum kim ca etat bhavatā na jñāyate yathā nāvanītam hṛdayam brāhmaṇasya viparītam etat ubhayam kṣatriyasya vāc nāvanītī hṛdayam tīkṣṇa dhāram tat evam gate na śaktaḥ aham tīkṣṇa hṛdaya tvāt tam śāpam anyathā kartum yasmāt aduṣṭam annam dūṣayasi tasmāt anapatyaḥ bhaviṣyasi iti duṣṭe ca anne na eṣa mama śāpaḥ bhaviṣyati iti sādhayāmaḥ tāvat iti uktvā prātiṣṭhata uttaṅkaḥ te kuṇḍale gṛhītvā saḥ apaśyat pathi nagnam śramaṇam āgacchantam muhur muhur dṛśyamānam a dṛśyamānam ca etasmin antare sa śramaṇaḥ tvaramāṇaḥ upasṛtya te kuṇḍale gṛhītvā prādravat sa tat rūpam vihāya takṣaka rūpam kṛtvā sahasā dharaṇyām vivṛtam mahā bilam viveśa praviśya ca nāgān astuvat ebhiḥ ślokaiḥ ye airāvata rājānaḥ sarpāḥ samiti śobhanāḥ varṣantaḥ iva jīmūtāḥ sa vidyut pavana īritāḥ surūpāḥ ca virūpāḥ ca tathā kalmāṣa kuṇḍalāḥ āditya vat nāka pṛṣṭhe rejuḥ airāvata udbhavāḥ bahūni nāgavartmāni gaṅgāyāḥ tīre uttare icchet kaḥ arka aṃśu senāyām cartum airāvatam vinā śatāni aśītiḥ aṣṭau ca sahasrāṇi ca viṃśatiḥ sarpāṇām pragrahāḥ yānti dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ yat ejati aham airāvata jyeṣṭha bhrātṛbhyaḥ akaravam namaḥ yasya vāsaḥ kurukṣetre khāṇḍave ca abhavat sadā tam kādraveyam astauṣam kuṇḍala arthāya takṣakam takṣakaḥ ca aśvasenaḥ ca nityam sahacarau ubhau kurukṣetre nivasatām nadīm ikṣumatīm anu karavāṇi sadā ca aham namaḥ tasmai mahātmane tasmin ca tantre kṛṣṇāḥ sitāḥ ca tantavaḥ cakram ca apaśyat ṣaḍbhiḥ kumāraiḥ parivartyamānam puruṣam ca apaśyat darśanīyam sa tān sarvān tuṣṭāva ebhiḥ mantravāda ślokaiḥ trīṇi arpitāni atra śatāni madhye ṣaṣṭiḥ ca nityam carati dhruve asmin kṛṣṇān sitān ca eva vivartayantyau bhūtāni ajasram bhuvanāni ca eva kṛṣṇe vasānaḥ vasane mahātmā satya anṛte yaḥ vivinakti loke yaḥ vājinam garbham apām purāṇam vaiśvānaram vāhanam abhyupetaḥ namaḥ sadā asmai jagat īśvarāya lokatraya īśāya puraṃdarāya tatas saḥ enam puruṣaḥ prāha kim te priyam karavāṇi iti nāgāḥ me vaśam īyuḥ iti saḥ enam puruṣaḥ punar uvāca atha aśvāt dhamyamānāt sarva srotobhyaḥ sa dhūmāḥ arciṣaḥ agneḥ niṣpetuḥ tābhiḥ nāga lokaḥ dhūpitaḥ atha sa saṃbhramaḥ takṣakaḥ agni tejaḥ bhaya viṣaṇṇaḥ te kuṇḍale gṛhītvā sahasā sva bhavanāt niṣkramya uttaṅkam uvāca ete kuṇḍale pratigṛhṇātu bhavān iti kuṇḍale pratigṛhya acintayat adya tat puṇyakam upādhyāyinyāḥ dūram ca aham abhyāgataḥ eṣa tvām kṣaṇāt eva upādhyāya kulam prāpayiṣyati iti upādhyāyinī ca snātā keśān āvapayantī upaviṣṭā uttaṅkaḥ na āgacchati iti śāpāya asya manaḥ dadhe atha uttaṅkaḥ praviśya upādhyāyinīm abhyavādayat te ca asyai kuṇḍale prāyacchat sā ca enam pratyuvāca uttaṅka deśe kāle abhyāgataḥ manāk asi mayā na śaptaḥ tam upādhyāyaḥ pratyuvāca kim ciram kṛtam iti tam uttaṅkaḥ upādhyāyam pratyuvāca bhoḥ takṣakeṇa nāga rājena vighnaḥ kṛtaḥ asmin karmaṇi tena asmi nāga lokam nītaḥ tasmin ca tantre kṛṣṇāḥ sitāḥ ca tantavaḥ kim tat tatra ca mayā cakram dṛṣṭam dvādaśa aram ṣaṭ ca enam kumārāḥ parivartayanti puruṣaḥ ca api mayā dṛṣṭaḥ sa punar kaḥ aśvaḥ ca ati pramāṇa yuktaḥ sa ca api kaḥ pathi gacchatā mayā ṛṣabhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tam ca puruṣaḥ adhirūḍhaḥ uttaṅka asya ṛṣabhasya purīṣam bhakṣaya ye te striyau dhātā vidhātā ca ye ca te kṛṣṇāḥ sitāḥ ca tantavaḥ te rātri ahanī yat api tat cakram dvādaśa aram ṣaṭ kumārāḥ parivartayanti te ṛtavaḥ ṣaṭ saṃvatsaraḥ cakram yaḥ puruṣaḥ sa parjanyaḥ yaḥ aśvaḥ saḥ agniḥ yaḥ ṛṣabhaḥ tvayā pathi gacchatā dṛṣṭaḥ saḥ airāvataḥ nāga rājaḥ yaḥ ca enam adhirūḍhaḥ saḥ indraḥ yat api te purīṣam bhakṣitam tasya ṛṣabhasya tat amṛtam tad anugrahāt kuṇḍale gṛhītvā punar abhyāgataḥ asi śreyaḥ avāpsyasi iti saḥ upādhyāyena anujñātaḥ uttaṅkaḥ kruddhaḥ takṣakasya praticikīrṣamāṇaḥ hāstinapuram pratasthe purā takṣaśilātaḥ tam nivṛttam aparājitam samyak vijayinam dṛṣṭvā samantāt mantribhiḥ vṛtam tasmai jaya āśiṣaḥ pūrvam yathānyāyam prayujya saḥ uvāca enam vacaḥ kāle śabda saṃpannayā girā bālyāt iva anyat eva tvam kuruṣe nṛpa sattama āsām prajānām paripālanena svam kṣatra dharmam paripālayāmi prabrūhi vā kim kriyatām dvijendra śuśrūṣuḥ asmi adya vacaḥ tvadīyam saḥ evam uktaḥ tu nṛpa uttamena dvijottamaḥ puṇya kṛtām variṣṭhaḥ uvāca rājānam adīna sattvam svam eva kāryam nṛpateḥ ca yat tat kārya kālam ca manye aham vidhi dṛṣṭasya karmaṇaḥ tena hi anaparādhī sa daṣṭaḥ duṣṭa antarātmanā akāryam kṛtavān pāpaḥ yaḥ adaśat pitaram tava rājarṣi vaṃśa goptāram amara pratimam nṛpam jaghāna kāśyapam ca eva nyavartayata pāpa kṛt evam pituḥ ca apacitim gatavān tvam bhaviṣyasi karmaṇaḥ pṛthivīpāla mama yena durātmanā uttaṅka vākya haviṣā dīptaḥ agniḥ haviṣā yathā apṛcchat ca tadā rājā mantriṇaḥ svān su duḥkhitaḥ yadā eva pitaram vṛttam uttaṅkāt aśṛṇot tadā lomaharṣaṇa putraḥ ugraśravāḥ sūtaḥ paurāṇikaḥ naimiṣa araṇye śaunakasya kula pateḥ dvādaśa vārṣike satre ṛṣīn abhyāgatān upatasthe paurāṇikaḥ purāṇe kṛta śramaḥ sa tān kṛtāñjaliḥ uvāca kim aham bruvāṇi iti tam ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ paramam lomaharṣaṇe prakṣyāmaḥ tvām vakṣyasi ca naḥ śuśrūṣatām kathā yogam yaḥ asau divyāḥ kathāḥ veda devatā asura saṃkathāḥ dakṣaḥ dhṛta vrataḥ dhīmān śāstre ca āraṇyake guruḥ sarveṣām eva naḥ mānyaḥ sa tāvat pratipālyatām sūtaḥ uvāca tena pṛṣṭaḥ kathāḥ puṇyāḥ vakṣyāmi vividha āśrayāḥ saḥ atha vipra ṛṣabhaḥ kāryam kṛtvā sarvam yathākramam yatra brahmarṣayaḥ siddhāḥ te āsīnāḥ yata vratāḥ yajña āyatanam āśritya sūtaputra puraḥsarāḥ upaviṣṭeṣu upaviṣṭaḥ śaunakaḥ atha abravīt idam śaunakaḥ uvāca purāṇam akhilam tāta pitā te adhītavān purā purāṇe hi kathāḥ divyāḥ ādi vaṃśāḥ ca dhīmatām kathyante tāḥ purā asmābhiḥ śrutāḥ pūrvam pituḥ tava tatra vaṃśam aham pūrvam śrotum icchāmi bhārgavam kathayasva kathām etām kalyāḥ sma śravaṇe tava sūtaḥ uvāca yat adhītam purā samyak dvijaśreṣṭha mahātmabhiḥ vaiśaṃpāyana vipra ādyaiḥ taiḥ ca api kathitam purā tat tāvat śṛṇu yaḥ devaiḥ sa indraiḥ sa agni marut gaṇaiḥ pūjitaḥ pravaraḥ vaṃśaḥ bhṛgūṇām bhṛgu nandana imam vaṃśam aham brahman bhārgavam te mahā mune nigadāmi kathā yuktam purāṇa āśraya saṃyutam bhṛgoḥ su dayitaḥ putraḥ cyavanaḥ nāma bhārgavaḥ cyavanasya api dāyādaḥ pramatiḥ nāma dhārmikaḥ pramadvarāyām dharma ātmā tava pūrva pitāmahāt tapasvī ca yaśasvī ca śrutavān brahma vittamaḥ śaunakaḥ uvāca cyavana tvam parikhyātam tat mama ācakṣva pṛcchataḥ sūtaḥ uvāca bhṛgoḥ su dayitā bhāryā pulomā iti abhiviśrutā tasmin garbhe saṃbhṛte atha pulomāyām bhṛgūdvaha samaye sama śīlinyām dharmapatnyām yaśasvinaḥ abhiṣekāya niṣkrānte bhṛgau dharma bhṛtām vare āśramam tasya rakṣaḥ atha pulomā abhyājagāma ha tam praviśya āśramam dṛṣṭvā bhṛgoḥ bhāryām aninditām hṛcchayena samāviṣṭaḥ vicetāḥ samapadyata abhyāgatam tu tat rakṣaḥ pulomā cāru darśanā tām tu rakṣaḥ tatas brahman hṛcchayena abhipīḍitam dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭam abhūt tatra jihīrṣuḥ tām aninditām atha agni śaraṇe apaśyat jvalitam jātavedasam tam apṛcchat tatas rakṣaḥ pāvakam jvalitam tadā śaṃsa me kasya bhāryā iyam agne pṛṣṭaḥ ṛtena vai mayā hi iyam pūrva vṛtā bhāryā arthe varavarṇinī paścāt tu imām pitā prādāt bhṛgave anṛta kāriṇe sā iyam yadi vara ārohā bhṛgoḥ bhāryā rahaḥ gatā tathā satyam samākhyāhi jihīrṣāmi āśramāt imām mad purva bhāryām yat imām bhṛguḥ prāpa sumadhyamām śaṅkamānaḥ bhṛgoḥ bhāryām punar punar apṛcchata sākṣi vat puṇya pāpeṣu satyam brūhi kave vacaḥ mad pūrva bhāryā apahṛtā bhṛguṇā anṛta kāriṇā śrutvā tvattaḥ bhṛgoḥ bhāryām hariṣyāmi aham āśramāt jātavedaḥ paśyataḥ te vada satyām giram mama tasya tat vacanam śrutvā saptārciḥ duḥkhitaḥ bhṛśam bhītaḥ anṛtāt ca śāpāt ca bhṛgoḥ iti abravīt śanais sūtaḥ uvāca agneḥ atha vacaḥ śrutvā tat rakṣaḥ prajahāra tām brahman varāha rūpeṇa manaḥ māruta raṃhasā roṣāt mātuḥ cyutaḥ kukṣeḥ cyavanaḥ tena saḥ abhavat tam dṛṣṭvā mātuḥ udarāt cyutam āditya varcasam sā tam ādāya suśroṇī sasāra bhṛgunandanam cyavanam bhārgavam brahman pulomā duḥkha mūrcchitā tām dadarśa svayam brahmā sarva loka pitāmahaḥ rudatīm bāṣpa pūrṇa akṣīm bhṛgoḥ bhāryām aninditām sāntvayām āsa bhagavān vadhūm brahmā pitāmahaḥ aśru bindu udbhavā tasyāḥ prāvartata mahā nadī anuvartatī sṛtim tasyāḥ bhṛgoḥ patnyā yaśasvinaḥ tasyāḥ mārgam sṛtavatīm dṛṣṭvā tu saritam tadā nāma tasyāḥ tadā nadyāḥ cakre lokapitāmahaḥ vadhūsarā iti bhagavān cyavanasya āśramam prati saḥ evam cyavanaḥ jajñe bhṛgoḥ putraḥ pratāpavān tam dadarśa pitā tatra cyavanam tām ca bhāminīm sa pulomām tatas bhāryām papraccha kupitaḥ bhṛguḥ na hi tvām veda tat rakṣaḥ mad bhāryām cāru hāsinīm tat tvam ākhyāhi tam hi adya śaptum icchāmi aham ruṣā bibheti kaḥ na śāpāt me kasya ca ayam vyatikramaḥ tatas mām anayat rakṣaḥ krośantīm kurarīm iva sā aham tava sutasya asya tejasā parimokṣitā bhasmībhūtam ca tat rakṣaḥ mām utsṛjya papāta vai sūtaḥ uvāca iti śrutvā pulomāyāḥ bhṛguḥ parama manyumān śaśāpa agnim abhikruddhaḥ sarva bhakṣaḥ bhaviṣyasi sūtaḥ uvāca śaptaḥ tu bhṛguṇā vahniḥ kruddhaḥ vākyam atha abravīt kim idam sāhasam brahman kṛtavān asi sāṃpratam pṛṣṭaḥ yat abruvam satyam vyabhicāraḥ atra kaḥ mama pṛṣṭaḥ hi sākṣī yaḥ sākṣyam jānamānaḥ anyathā vadet sa pūrvān ātmanaḥ sapta kule hanyāt tathā parān yaḥ ca kārya artha tattva jñaḥ jānamānaḥ na bhāṣate śaktaḥ aham api śaptum tvām mānyāḥ tu brāhmaṇāḥ mama yogena bahudhā ātmānam kṛtvā tiṣṭhāmi mūrtiṣu āpaḥ deva gaṇāḥ sarve āpaḥ pitṛ gaṇāḥ tathā darśaḥ ca paurṇamāsaḥ ca devānām pitṛbhiḥ saha devatāḥ pitaraḥ tasmāt pitaraḥ ca api devatāḥ ekībhūtāḥ ca pūjyante pṛthaktvena ca parvasu tridaśānām pitṝṇām ca mukham evam aham smṛtaḥ amāvāsyām ca pitaraḥ paurṇamāsyām ca devatāḥ sarva bhakṣaḥ katham teṣām bhaviṣyāmi mukham tu aham cintayitvā tatas vahniḥ cakre saṃhāram ātmanaḥ niroṃkāra vaṣaṭkārāḥ svadhā svāhā vivarjitāḥ vinā agninā prajāḥ sarvāḥ tatas āsan su duḥkhitāḥ agni nāśāt kriyā bhraṃśāt bhrāntāḥ lokāḥ trayaḥ anaghāḥ atha ṛṣayaḥ ca devāḥ ca brahmāṇam upagamya tu agneḥ āvedayan śāpam kriyā saṃhāram eva ca bhṛguṇā vai mahābhāga śaptaḥ agniḥ kāraṇa antare katham deva mukhaḥ bhūtvā yajña bhāga agra bhuj tathā śrutvā tu tat vacaḥ teṣām agnim āhūya lokakṛt uvāca vacanam ślakṣṇam bhūta bhāvanam avyayam lokānām iha sarveṣām tvam kartā ca antaḥ eva ca tvam dhārayasi lokān trīn kriyāṇām ca pravartakaḥ kasmāt evam vimūḍhaḥ tvam īśvaraḥ san hutāśanaḥ na tvam sarva śarīreṇa sarva bhakṣa tvam eṣyasi upādāne arciṣaḥ yāḥ te sarvam dhakṣyanti tāḥ śikhin yathā sūrya aṃśubhiḥ spṛṣṭam sarvam śuci vibhāvyate sva tejasā eva tam śāpam kuru satyam ṛṣeḥ vibho devānām ca ātmanaḥ bhāgam gṛhāṇa tvam mukhe hutam jagāma śāsanam kartum devasya parameṣṭhinaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca yathāpūrvam kriyāḥ sarvāḥ pracakrire divi devāḥ mumudire bhūta saṃghāḥ ca laukikāḥ agniḥ ca paramām prītim avāpa hata kalmaṣaḥ evam eṣa purāvṛttaḥ itihāsaḥ agni śāpa jaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca sukanyāyām mahātmānam pramatim dīpta tejasam pramatiḥ tu rurum nāma ghṛtācyām samajījanat ruruḥ pramadvarāyām tu śunakam samajījanat vistareṇa pravakṣyāmi tat śṛṇu tvam aśeṣatas ṛṣiḥ āsīt mahān pūrvam tapaḥ vidyā samanvitaḥ sthūlakeśaḥ iti khyātaḥ sarva bhūta hite rataḥ etasmin eva kāle tu menakāyām prajajñivān gandharva rājaḥ vipra ṛṣe viśvāvasuḥ iti śrutaḥ athā apsarāḥ menakā sā tam garbham bhṛgu nandana utsasarja yathākālam sthūlakeśa āśramam prati utsṛjya ca eva tam garbham nadyāḥ tīre jagāma ha kanyām amara garbha ābhām jvalantīm iva ca śriyā tām dadarśa samutsṛṣṭām nadī tīre mahān ṛṣiḥ sa tām dṛṣṭvā tadā kanyām sthūlakeśaḥ dvijottamaḥ jagrāha atha muni śreṣṭhaḥ kṛpā āviṣṭaḥ pupoṣa ca vavṛdhe sā varārohā tasya āśrama pade śubhā pramadābhyaḥ varā sā tu sarva rūpa guṇa anvitā tatas pramadvarā iti asyāḥ nāma cakre mahān ṛṣiḥ tām āśrama pade tasya ruruḥ dṛṣṭvā pramadvarām babhūva kila dharma ātmā madana anugata ātmavān pitaram sakhibhiḥ saḥ atha vācayām āsa bhārgavaḥ pramatiḥ ca abhyayāt śrutvā sthūlakeśam yaśasvinam tatas prādāt pitā kanyām rurave tām pramadvarām sakhībhiḥ krīḍatī sārdham sā kanyā varavarṇinī padā ca enam samākrāmat mumūrṣuḥ kāla coditā sa tasyāḥ saṃpramattāyāḥ coditaḥ kāladharmaṇā viṣa upaliptān daśanān bhṛśam aṅge nyapātayat sā daṣṭā sahasā bhūmau patitā gata cetanā vyasuḥ a prekṣaṇīyā api prekṣaṇīyatama ākṛtiḥ dadarśa tām pitā ca eva te ca eva anye tapasvinaḥ viceṣṭamānām patitām bhū tale padma varcasam tatas sarve dvijavarāḥ samājagmuḥ kṛpā anvitāḥ svastyātreyaḥ mahā jānuḥ kuśikaḥ śaṅkha mekhalaḥ bhāradvājaḥ kauṇakutsaḥ ārṣṭiṣeṇaḥ atha gautamaḥ tām te kanyām vyasum dṛṣṭvā bhujagasya viṣa arditām ruruduḥ kṛpayā āviṣṭāḥ ruruḥ tu ārtaḥ bahis yayau sūtaḥ uvāca teṣu tatra upaviṣṭeṣu brāhmaṇeṣu samantataḥ ruruḥ cukrośa gahanam vanam gatvā su duḥkhitaḥ śete sā bhuvi tanvaṅgī mama śoka vivardhinī bāndhavānām ca sarveṣām kim nu duḥkham atas param samyak ārādhitāḥ tena saṃjīvatu mama priyā yathā janma prabhṛti vai yata ātmā aham dhṛta vrataḥ deva dūtaḥ uvāca abhidhatse ha yat vācā ruro duḥkhena tat mṛṣā gata āyuḥ eṣā kṛpaṇā gandharva apsarasoḥ sutā tasmāt śoke manaḥ tāta mā kṛthāḥ tvam katham cana upāyaḥ ca atra vihitaḥ pūrvam devaiḥ mahātmabhiḥ tam yadi icchasi kartum tvam prāpsyasi imām pramadvarām kariṣye tam tathā śrutvā trātum arhati mām bhavān deva dūtaḥ uvāca śṛṅgāra rūpa ābharaṇā uttiṣṭhatu mama priyā sūtaḥ uvāca samuttiṣṭhatu kalyāṇī mṛtā eva yadi manyase sūtaḥ uvāca etat dṛṣṭam bhaviṣye hi ruroḥ uttama tejasaḥ sa labdhvā durlabhām bhāryām padma kiñjalka saprabhām vratam cakre vināśāya jihmagānām dhṛta vrataḥ sa dṛṣṭvā jihmagān sarvān tīvra kopa samanvitaḥ abhihanti yathāsannam gṛhya praharaṇam sadā śayānam tatra ca apaśyat ḍuṇḍubham vayasā anvitam tatas udyamya daṇḍam sa kāla daṇḍa upamam tadā abhyaghnat ruṣitaḥ vipraḥ tam uvāca atha ḍuṇḍubhaḥ saṃrambhāt tat kimartham mām abhihaṃsi ruṣā anvitaḥ mama prāṇa samā bhāryā daṣṭā āsīt bhujagena ha tatas aham tvām jighāṃsāmi jīvitena vimokṣyase ḍuṇḍubhaḥ uvāca ḍuṇḍubhān ahi gandhena na tvam hiṃsitum arhasi eka anarthān pṛthak arthān eka duḥkhān pṛthak sukhān ḍuṇḍubhān dharma vid bhūtvā na tvam hiṃsitum arhasi sūtaḥ uvāca na avadhīt bhaya saṃvignaḥ ṛṣim matvā atha ḍuṇḍubham uvāca ca enam bhagavān ruruḥ saṃśamayan iva kāmayā bhujaga brūhi kaḥ asi imām vikriyām gataḥ ḍuṇḍubhaḥ uvāca aham purā ruro nāmnā ṛṣiḥ āsam sahasrapād ḍuṇḍubhaḥ uvāca sakhā babhūva me pūrvam khagamaḥ nāma vai dvijaḥ bhṛśam saṃśita vāc tāta tapaḥ bala samanvitaḥ sa mayā krīḍatā bālye kṛtvā tārṇam atha uragam labdhvā ca sa punar saṃjñām mām uvāca tapodhanaḥ yathāvīryaḥ tvayā sarpaḥ kṛtaḥ ayam mad bibhīṣayā tasya aham tapasaḥ vīryam jānamānaḥ tapodhana prayataḥ saṃbhramāt ca eva prāñjaliḥ praṇataḥ sthitaḥ sakhā iti hasatā idam te narma artham vai kṛtam mayā saḥ atha mām abravīt dṛṣṭvā bhṛśam udvigna cetasam muhur uṣṇam viniḥśvasya su saṃbhrāntaḥ tapodhanaḥ na anṛtam vai mayā proktam bhavitā idam katham cana yat tu vakṣyāmi te vākyam śṛṇu tat me dhṛta vrata tam dṛṣṭvā śāpa mokṣaḥ te bhavitā nacirāt iva sa tvam ruruḥ iti khyātaḥ pramateḥ ātmajaḥ śuciḥ ahiṃsā paramaḥ dharmaḥ sarva prāṇabhṛtām smṛtaḥ tasmāt prāṇabhṛtaḥ sarvān na hiṃsyāt brāhmaṇaḥ kva cit brāhmaṇaḥ saumyaḥ eva iha jāyata iti parā śrutiḥ ahiṃsā satya vacanam kṣamā ca iti viniścitam brāhmaṇasya paraḥ dharmaḥ vedānām dharaṇāt api daṇḍa dhāraṇam ugra tvam prajānām paripālanam tat idam kṣatriyasya āsīt karma vai śṛṇu me ruro janamejayasya dharma ātman sarpāṇām hiṃsanam purā paritrāṇam ca bhītānām sarpāṇām brāhmaṇāt api tapaḥ vīrya bala upetāt veda vedāṅga pāragāt sarpāḥ vā hiṃsitāḥ tāta kimartham dvijasattama kimartham mokṣitāḥ ca eva pannagāḥ tena śaṃsa me āstīkena tat ācakṣva śrotum icchāmi aśeṣatas ṛṣiḥ uvāca śroṣyasi tvam ruro sarvam āstīka caritam mahat brāhmaṇānām kathayatām iti uktvā antaradhīyata sūtaḥ uvāca tam ṛṣim draṣṭum anvicchan saṃśrāntaḥ nyapatat bhuvi labdha saṃjñaḥ ruruḥ ca ayāt tat ca ācakhyau pituḥ tadā pitā ca asya tat ākhyānam pṛṣṭaḥ sarvam nyavedayat śaunakaḥ uvāca kimartham rāja śārdūlaḥ sa rājā janamejayaḥ sarpa satreṇa sarpāṇām gataḥ antam tat vadasva me āstīkaḥ ca dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ kimartham japatām varaḥ mokṣayām āsa bhujagān dīptāt tasmāt hutāśanāt kasya putraḥ sa rājā āsīt sarpa satram yaḥ āharat sūtaḥ uvāca sarvam etat aśeṣeṇa śṛṇu me vadatām vara śaunakaḥ uvāca śrotum icchāmi aśeṣeṇa kathām etām manoramām āstīkasya purāṇasya brāhmaṇasya yaśasvinaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca itihāsam imam vṛddhāḥ purāṇam paricakṣate kṛṣṇadvaipāyana proktam naimiṣa araṇya vāsinaḥ pūrvam pracoditaḥ sūtaḥ pitā me lomaharṣaṇaḥ śiṣyaḥ vyāsasya medhāvī brāhmaṇaiḥ idam uktavān idam āstīkam ākhyānam tubhyam śaunaka pṛcchate āstīkasya pitā hi āsīt prajāpati samaḥ prabhuḥ brahmacārī yata āhāraḥ tapasi ugre rataḥ sadā jaratkāruḥ iti khyātaḥ ūrdhvaretāḥ mahān ṛṣiḥ yāyāvarāṇām dharma jñaḥ pravaraḥ saṃśita vrataḥ aṭamānaḥ kadā cit sa svān dadarśa pitāmahān tān abravīt sa dṛṣṭvā eva jaratkāruḥ pitāmahān vīraṇa stambake lagnāḥ sarvatas paribhakṣite mūṣakena nigūḍhena garte asmin nitya vāsinā pitaraḥ ūcuḥ yāyāvarāḥ nāma vayam ṛṣayaḥ saṃśita vratāḥ asmākam saṃtatiḥ tu ekaḥ jaratkāruḥ iti śrutaḥ mandabhāgyaḥ alpabhāgyānām tapaḥ eva samāsthitaḥ na sa putrān janayitum dārān mūḍhaḥ cikīrṣati anāthāḥ tena nāthena yathā duṣkṛtinaḥ tathā jñātum icchāmahe brahman kaḥ bhavān iha dhiṣṭhitaḥ brūta kim karavāṇi adya jaratkāruḥ aham svayam pitaraḥ ūcuḥ yatasva yatnavān tāta saṃtānāya kulasya naḥ tām gatim prāpnuvanti iha putriṇaḥ yām vrajanti ha tat dāra grahaṇe yatnam saṃtatyām ca manaḥ kuru na dārān vai kariṣyāmi sadā me bhāvitam manaḥ bhavatām tu hita arthāya kariṣye dāra saṃgraham bhaikṣa vat tām aham kanyām upayaṃsye vidhānataḥ daridrāya hi me bhāryām kaḥ dāsyati viśeṣataḥ pratigrahīṣye bhikṣām tu yadi kaḥ cit pradāsyati evam dārakriyā hetoḥ prayatiṣye pitāmahāḥ śāśvatam sthānam āsādya modantām pitaraḥ mama sūtaḥ uvāca tatas niveśāya tadā sa vipraḥ saṃśita vrataḥ mahīm cacāra dāra arthī na ca dārān avindata sa kadā cit vanam gatvā vipraḥ pitṛ vacaḥ smaran cukrośa kanyā bhikṣā arthī tisraḥ vācaḥ śanais iva tam vāsukiḥ pratyagṛhṇāt udyamya bhaginīm tadā sanāmnīm udyatām bhāryām gṛhṇīyām iti tasya hi tam uvāca mahā prājñaḥ jaratkāruḥ mahā tapāḥ kiṃnāmnī bhaginī iyam te brūhi satyam bhujaṃgama vāsukiḥ uvāca tvad artham rakṣitā pūrvam pratīccha imām dvijottama sūtaḥ uvāca mātrā hi bhujagāḥ śaptāḥ pūrvam brahma vidām vara sa ca tām pratijagrāha vidhi dṛṣṭena karmaṇā āstīkaḥ nāma putraḥ ca tasyām jajñe mahātmanaḥ tapasvī ca mahātmā ca veda vedāṅga pāragaḥ samaḥ sarvasya lokasya pitṛ mātṛ bhaya apahaḥ atha kālasya mahataḥ pāṇḍaveyaḥ narādhipaḥ ājahāra mahā yajñam sarpa satram iti śrutiḥ mocayām āsa tam śāpam āstīkaḥ su mahā yaśāḥ nāgān ca mātulān ca eva tathā ca anyān sa bāndhavān pitṝn ca tārayām āsa saṃtatyā tapasā tathā devān ca tarpayām āsa yajñaiḥ vividha dakṣiṇaiḥ ṛṣīn ca brahmacaryeṇa saṃtatyā ca pitāmahān apahṛtya gurum bhāram pitṝṇām saṃśita vrataḥ jaratkāruḥ gataḥ svargam sahitaḥ svaiḥ pitāmahaiḥ āstīkam ca sutam prāpya dharmam ca anuttamam muniḥ jaratkāruḥ su mahatā kālena svargam īyivān etat ākhyānam āstīkam yathāvat kīrtitam mayā prabrūhi bhṛguśārdūla kim bhūyas kathyatām iti śaunakaḥ uvāca saute kathaya tām etām vistareṇa kathām punar āstīkasya kaveḥ sādhoḥ śuśrūṣā paramā hi naḥ madhuram kathyate saumya ślakṣṇa akṣara padam tvayā prīyāmahe bhṛśam tāta pitā iva idam prabhāṣase asmad śuśrūṣaṇe nityam pitā hi nirataḥ tava ācaṣṭa etat yathākhyānam pitā te tvam tathā vada sūtaḥ uvāca āyuṣyam idam ākhyānam āstīkam kathayāmi te yathā śrutam kathayataḥ sakāśāt vai pituḥ mayā te bhārye kaśyapasya āstām kadrūḥ ca vinatā ca ha prādāt tābhyām varam prītaḥ prajāpati samaḥ patiḥ kaśyapaḥ dharma patnībhyām mudā paramayā yutaḥ vara atisargam śrutvā eva kaśyapāt uttamam ca te harṣāt apratimām prītim prāpatuḥ sma vara striyau vavre kadrūḥ sutān nāgān sahasram tulya tejasaḥ evam astu iti tam ca āha kaśyapam vinatā tadā kṛtakṛtyā tu vinatā labdhvā vīrya adhikau sutau kadrūḥ ca labdhvā putrāṇām sahasram tulya tejasām te bhārye vara saṃhṛṣṭe kaśyapaḥ vanam āviśat kālena mahatā kadrūḥ aṇḍānām daśatīḥ daśa janayām āsa vipra indra dve aṇḍe vinatā tadā tayoḥ aṇḍāni nidadhuḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ paricārikāḥ sa upasvedeṣu bhāṇḍeṣu pañca varṣa śatāni ca tatas pañcaśate kāle kadrū putrāḥ viniḥsṛtāḥ aṇḍābhyām vinatāyāḥ tu mithunam na vyadṛśyata tatas putra arthiṇī devī vrīḍitā sā tapasvinī aṇḍam bibheda vinatā tatra putram adṛkṣata pūrva ardha kāya saṃpannam itareṇa a prakāśa tā sa putraḥ roṣa saṃpannaḥ śaśāpa enām iti śrutiḥ yaḥ aham evam kṛtaḥ mātar tvayā lobha parītayā śarīreṇa asamagraḥ adya tasmāt dāsī bhaviṣyasi pañca varṣa śatāni asyāḥ yayā vispardhase saha eṣa ca tvām sutaḥ mātar dāsya tvāt mokṣayiṣyati yadi enam api mātar tvam mām iva aṇḍa vibhedanāt na kariṣyasi adeham vā vyaṅgam vā api tapasvinam viśiṣṭa balam īpsantyā pañca varṣa śatāt paras evam śaptvā tatas putraḥ vinatām antarikṣa gaḥ garuḍaḥ api yathākālam jajñe pannaga sūdanaḥ sa jāta mātraḥ vinatām parityajya kham āviśat vidhātrā bhṛgu śārdūla kṣudhitasya bubhukṣataḥ sūtaḥ uvāca apaśyatām samāyāntam uccaiḥśravasam antikāt yam tam deva gaṇāḥ sarve hṛṣṭa rūpāḥ apūjayan mahā ogha balam aśvānām uttamam javatām varam śrīmantam ajaram divyam sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣitam śaunakaḥ uvāca yatra jajñe mahā vīryaḥ saḥ aśvarājaḥ mahā dyutiḥ sūtaḥ uvāca ākṣipantam prabhām bhānoḥ sva śṛṅgaiḥ kāñcana ujjvalaiḥ nākam āvṛtya tiṣṭhantam ucchrayeṇa mahā girim nānā pataga saṃghaiḥ ca nāditam su manoharaiḥ tasya pṛṣṭham upāruhya bahu ratna ācitam śubham te mantrayitum ārabdhāḥ tatra āsīnāḥ divaukasaḥ amṛta arthe samāgamya tapaḥ niyama saṃsthitāḥ tatra nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ brahmāṇam idam abravīt sarva oṣadhīḥ samāvāpya sarva ratnāni ca eva hi sūtaḥ uvāca tatas abhra śikhara ākāraiḥ giri śṛṅgaiḥ alaṃkṛtam mandaram parvata varam latā jāla samāvṛtam nānā vihaga saṃghuṣṭam nānā daṃṣṭri samākulam ekādaśa sahasrāṇi yojanānām samucchritam tam uddhartum na śaktāḥ vai sarve deva gaṇāḥ tadā viṣṇum āsīnam abhyetya brahmāṇam ca idam abruvan bhavantau atra kurutām buddhim naiḥśreyasīm parām mandara uddharaṇe yatnaḥ kriyatām ca hitāya naḥ tathā iti ca abravīt viṣṇuḥ brahmaṇā saha bhārgava nārāyaṇena ca api uktaḥ tasmin karmaṇi vīryavān tam ūcuḥ amṛta arthāya nirmathiṣyāmahe jalam apāṃpatiḥ athā uvāca mama api aṃśaḥ bhavet tatas soḍhāsmi vipulam mardam mandara bhramaṇāt iti ūcuḥ ca kūrma rājānam akūpāram sura asurāḥ manthānam mandaram kṛtvā tathā netram ca vāsukim ekam antam upāśliṣṭāḥ nāga rājñaḥ mahā asurāḥ vibudhāḥ sahitāḥ sarve yatas puccham tatas sthitāḥ vāsukeḥ atha nāgasya sahasā ākṣipyataḥ suraiḥ sa dhūmāḥ sa arciṣaḥ vātāḥ niṣpetuḥ asakṛt mukhāt te dhūma saṃghāḥ saṃbhūtāḥ megha saṃghāḥ sa vidyutaḥ abhyavarṣan sura gaṇān śrama saṃtāpa karśitān tasmāt ca giri kūṭa agrāt pracyutāḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭayaḥ sura asura gaṇān mālyaiḥ sarvatas samavākiran babhūva atra mahā ghoṣaḥ mahā megha rava upamaḥ tatra nānā jalacarāḥ viniṣpiṣṭāḥ mahā adriṇā vilayam samupājagmuḥ śataśas lavaṇāmbhasi vāruṇāni ca bhūtāni vividhāni mahīdharaḥ pātāla tala vāsīni vilayam samupānayat tasmin ca bhrāmyamāṇe adrau saṃghṛṣyantaḥ parasparam nyapatan pataga upetāḥ parvata agrāt mahā drumāḥ teṣām saṃgharṣa jaḥ ca agniḥ arcirbhiḥ prajvalan muhur dadāha kuñjarān ca eva siṃhān ca eva viniḥsṛtān vigata asūni sarvāṇi sattvāni vividhāni ca vāriṇā megha jena indraḥ śamayām āsa sarvatas tatas nānāvidhāḥ tatra susruvuḥ sāgara ambhasi mahā drumāṇām niryāsāḥ bahavaḥ ca oṣadhī rasāḥ teṣām amṛta vīryāṇām rasānām payasā eva ca amara tvam surāḥ jagmuḥ kāñcanasya ca niḥsravāt rasa uttamaiḥ vimiśram ca tatas kṣīrāt abhūt ghṛtam tatas brahmāṇam āsīnam devāḥ vara dam abruvan śrāntāḥ sma su bhṛśam brahman nā udbhavati amṛtam ca tat ṛte nārāyaṇam devam daityāḥ nāga uttamāḥ tathā tatas nārāyaṇam devam brahmā vacanam abravīt vidhatsva eṣām balam viṣṇo bhavān atra parāyaṇam viṣṇuḥ uvāca balam dadāmi sarveṣām karma etat ye samāsthitāḥ kṣobhyatām kalaśaḥ sarvaiḥ mandaraḥ parivartyatām sūtaḥ uvāca nārāyaṇa vacaḥ śrutvā balinaḥ te mahodadheḥ tat payaḥ sahitāḥ bhūyas cakrire bhṛśam ākulam tatas śata sahasra aṃśuḥ samānaḥ iva sāgarāt prasanna bhās samutpannaḥ somaḥ śītāṃśuḥ ujjvalaḥ śrīḥ anantaram utpannā ghṛtāt pāṇḍura vāsinī surā devī samutpannā turagaḥ pāṇḍuraḥ tathā marīci vikacaḥ śrīmān śrīḥ surā ca eva somaḥ ca turagaḥ ca manaḥ javaḥ yatas devāḥ tatas jagmuḥ āditya patham āśritāḥ śvetam kamaṇḍalum bibhrat amṛtam yatra tiṣṭhati etat ati adbhutam dṛṣṭvā dānavānām samutthitaḥ tatas nārāyaṇaḥ māyām āsthitaḥ mohinīm prabhuḥ strī rūpam adbhutam kṛtvā dānavān abhisaṃśritaḥ dānava daiteyāḥ sarve tad gata mānasāḥ sūtaḥ uvāca atha āvaraṇa mukhyāni nānā praharaṇāni ca pragṛhya abhyadravan devān sahitāḥ daitya dānavāḥ tatas tat amṛtam devaḥ viṣṇuḥ ādāya vīryavān tatas deva gaṇāḥ sarve papuḥ tat amṛtam tadā viṣṇoḥ sakāśāt saṃprāpya saṃbhrame tumule sati tatas pibatsu tad kālam deveṣu amṛtam īpsitam rāhuḥ vibudha rūpeṇa dānavaḥ prāpibat tadā tasya kaṇṭham anuprāpte dānavasya amṛte tadā ākhyātam candra sūryābhyām surāṇām hita kāmyayā tat śaila śṛṅga pratimam dānavasya śiraḥ mahat śāśvataḥ candra sūryābhyām grasati adyā api ca eva tau vihāya bhagavān ca api strī rūpam atulam hariḥ tatas pravṛttaḥ saṃgrāmaḥ samīpe lavaṇāmbhasaḥ surāṇām asurāṇām ca sarva ghorataraḥ mahān prāsāḥ su vipulāḥ tīkṣṇāḥ nyapatanta sahasraśas tomarāḥ ca su tīkṣṇa agrāḥ śastrāṇi vividhāni ca asi śakti gadā rugṇāḥ nipetuḥ dharaṇī tale chinnāni paṭṭiśaiḥ ca api śirāṃsi yudhi dāruṇe tapta kāñcana jālāni nipetuḥ aniśam tadā rudhireṇa avalipta aṅgāḥ nihatāḥ ca mahā asurāḥ adrīṇām iva kūṭāni dhātu raktāni śerate hāhākāraḥ samabhavat tatra tatra sahasraśas parighaiḥ ca āyasaiḥ pītaiḥ saṃnikarṣe ca muṣṭibhiḥ nighnatām samare anyonyam śabdaḥ divam iva aspṛśat vyaśrūyanta mahā ghorāḥ śabdāḥ tatra samantataḥ cintayām āsa vai cakram viṣṇuḥ dānava sūdanam atha ambarāt bhaya jananāḥ prapedire sa pādapāḥ bahuvidha megha rūpiṇaḥ tatas mahī pravicalitā sa kānanā mahā adri pāta abhihatā samantataḥ parasparam bhṛśam abhigarjatām muhur raṇa ajire bhṛśam abhisaṃpravartite tatas mahīm lavaṇa jalam ca sāgaram mahā asurāḥ praviviśuḥ arditāḥ suraiḥ sūtaḥ uvāca etat te sarvam ākhyātam amṛtam mathitam yathā yatra saḥ aśvaḥ samutpannaḥ śrīmān atula vikramaḥ yam niśāmya tadā kadrūḥ vinatām idam abravīt uccaiḥśravāḥ nu kiṃvarṇaḥ bhadre jānīhi māciram śvetaḥ eva aśvarājaḥ ayam kim vā tvam manyase śubhe kadrūḥ uvāca kṛṣṇa vālam aham manye hayam enam śuci smite ehi sārdham mayā dīvya dāsī bhāvāya bhāmini sūtaḥ uvāca evam te samayam kṛtvā dāsī bhāvāya vai mithas jagmatuḥ sva gṛhān eva śvas drakṣyāvaḥ iti sma ha tatas putra sahasram tu kadrūḥ jihmam cikīrṣatī ājñāpayām āsa tadā vālāḥ bhūtvā añjana prabhāḥ āviśadhvam hayam kṣipram dāsī na syām aham yathā tat vākyam na anvapadyanta tān śaśāpa bhujaṃgamān janamejayasya rājarṣeḥ pāṇḍaveyasya dhīmataḥ śāpam enam tu śuśrāva svayam eva pitāmahaḥ atikrūram samuddiṣṭam kadrvāḥ daivāt atīva hi sārdham deva gaṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ vācam tām anvamodata bahu tvam prekṣya sarpāṇām prajānām hita kāmyayā tigma vīrya viṣāḥ hi ete dandaśūkāḥ mahā balāḥ teṣām tīkṣṇa viṣa tvāt hi prajānām ca hitāya vai prādāt vidyām kāśyapāya mahātmane sūtaḥ uvāca tatas rajanyām vyuṣṭāyām prabhāte udite ravau amarṣite su saṃrabdhe dāsye kṛta paṇe tadā dadṛśāte tadā tatra samudram nidhim ambhasām timiṃgila jhaṣa ākīrṇam makaraiḥ āvṛtam tathā sattvaiḥ ca bahu sāhasraiḥ nānā rūpaiḥ samāvṛtam ugraiḥ nityam anādhṛṣyam kūrma grāha samākulam ākaram sarva ratnānām ālayam varuṇasya ca nāgānām ālayam ramyam uttamam saritām patim pātāla jvalana āvāsam asurāṇām ca bandhanam bhayaṃkaram ca sattvānām payasām nidhim arṇavam śubham divyam amartyānām amṛtasya ākaram param gām vindatā bhagavatā govindena amita ojasā varāha rūpiṇā ca antar vikṣobhita jala āvilam brahmarṣiṇā ca tapatā varṣāṇām śatam atriṇā an āsādita gādham ca pātāla talam avyayam yuga ādi kāla śayanam viṣṇoḥ amita tejasaḥ agādha pāram vistīrṇam aprameyam saritpatim abhisāryamāṇam aniśam dadṛśāte mahā arṇavam vistīrṇam dadṛśatuḥ ambara prakāśam te agādham nidhim urum ambhasām anantam pātāla jvalana śikhā vidīpitam tam paśyantyau drutam abhipetatuḥ tadānīm sūtaḥ uvāca nyapatat turaga abhyāśe nacirāt iva śīghra gā niśāmya ca bahūn vālān kṛṣṇān puccham samāśritān vinatām viṣaṇṇa vadanām kadrūḥ dāsye nyayojayat tatas sā vinatā tasmin paṇitena parājitā abhavat duḥkha saṃtaptā dāsī bhāvam samāsthitā vinā mātrā mahā tejāḥ vidārya aṇḍam ajāyata pravṛddhaḥ sahasā pakṣī mahā kāyaḥ nabhaḥ gataḥ tam dṛṣṭvā śaraṇam jagmuḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ vibhāvasum praṇipatya abruvan ca enam āsīnam viśva rūpiṇam agne mā tvam pravardhiṣṭhāḥ kaccit naḥ na didhakṣasi na etat evam yathā yūyam manyadhvam asura ardanāḥ sūtaḥ uvāca adūrāt abhyupetya enam devāḥ sa ṛṣi gaṇāḥ tadā tvam ṛṣiḥ tvam mahābhāgaḥ tvam devaḥ pataga īśvaraḥ tapaḥ śrutam sarvam ahīna kīrte evam stutaḥ suparṇaḥ tu devaiḥ sa ṛṣi gaṇaiḥ tadā tejasaḥ pratisaṃhāram ātmanaḥ sa cakāra ha sūtaḥ uvāca tatas kāma gamaḥ pakṣī mahā vīryaḥ mahā balaḥ mātuḥ antikam āgacchat param tīram mahā udadheḥ atīva duḥkha saṃtaptā dāsī bhāvam upāgatā tatas kadā cit vinatām pravaṇām putra saṃnidhau kāle āhūya vacanam kadrūḥ idam abhāṣata nāgānām ālayam bhadre su ramyam ramaṇīyakam tatas suparṇa mātā tām avahat sarpa mātaram pannagān garuḍaḥ ca api mātuḥ vacana coditaḥ sūrya raśmi parītāḥ ca mūrcchitāḥ pannagāḥ abhavan tad avasthān sutān dṛṣṭvā kadrūḥ śakram atha astuvat sarpāṇām sūrya taptānām vāriṇā tvam plavaḥ bhava īśaḥ hi asi payaḥ sraṣṭum tvam analpam puraṃdara tvam vajram atulam ghoram ghoṣavān tvam balāhakaḥ sraṣṭā tvam eva lokānām saṃhartā ca aparājitaḥ tvam jyotiḥ sarva bhūtānām tvam ādityaḥ vibhāvasuḥ tvam mahat bhūtam āścaryam tvam rājā tvam sura uttamaḥ tvam viṣṇuḥ tvam sahasra akṣaḥ tvam devaḥ tvam parāyaṇam tvam sarvam amṛtam deva tvam somaḥ parama arcitaḥ tvam muhūrtaḥ tithiḥ ca tvam lavaḥ tvam vai punar kṣaṇaḥ śuklaḥ tvam bahulaḥ ca eva kalā kāṣṭhā truṭiḥ tathā abhiṣṭutaḥ pibasi ca somam adhvare vaṣaṭkṛtāni api ca havīṃṣi bhūtaye sūtaḥ uvāca evam stutaḥ tadā kadrvā bhagavān harivāhanaḥ nīla jīmūta saṃghātaiḥ vyoma sarvam samāvṛṇot saṃghātitam iva ākāśam jaladaiḥ su mahā adbhutaiḥ saṃpranṛttam iva ākāśam dhārā ūrmibhiḥ anekaśas nāgānām uttamaḥ harśaḥ tadā varṣati vāsave sūtaḥ uvāca suparṇena uhyamānāḥ te jagmuḥ tam deśam āśu vai sāgara ambu parikṣiptam pakṣi saṃgha nināditam upajighradbhiḥ ākāśam vṛkṣaiḥ malayajaiḥ api śobhitam puṣpa varṣāṇi muñcadbhiḥ māruta uddhutaiḥ kiradbhiḥ iva tatrasthān nāgān puṣpa ambu vṛṣṭibhiḥ manaḥ saṃharṣaṇam puṇyam gandharva apsarasām priyam nānā pakṣi rutam ramyam kadru putra praharṣaṇam tat te vanam samāsādya vijahruḥ pannagāḥ mudā abruvan ca mahā vīryam suparṇam pataga uttamam vaha asmān aparam dvīpam su ramyam vipula udakam sa vicintya abravīt pakṣī mātaram vinatām tadā kim kāraṇam mayā mātar kartavyam sarpa bhāṣitam dāsī bhūtā asmi anāryāyāḥ bhaginyāḥ pataga uttama paṇam vitatham āsthāya sarpaiḥ upadhinā kṛtam sūtaḥ uvāca tasmin tu kathite mātrā kāraṇe gaganecaraḥ uvāca vacanam sarpān tena duḥkhena duḥkhitaḥ kim āhṛtya viditvā vā kim vā kṛtvā iha pauruṣam dāsyāt vaḥ vipramucyeyam satyam śaṃsata lelihāḥ śrutvā tam abruvan sarpāḥ āhara amṛtam ojasā sūtaḥ uvāca samudra kukṣau ekānte niṣāda ālayam uttamam sahasrāṇām anekānām tān bhuktvā amṛtam ānaya na tu te brāhmaṇam hantum kāryā buddhiḥ katham cana avadhyaḥ sarva bhūtānām brāhmaṇaḥ hi anala upamaḥ bhūtānām agra bhuj vipraḥ varṇa śreṣṭhaḥ pitā guruḥ garuḍaḥ uvāca yathā aham abhijānīyām brāhmaṇam lakṣaṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ yaḥ te kaṇṭham anuprāptaḥ nigīrṇam baḍiśam yathā dahet aṅgāra vat putra tam vidyāt brāhmaṇa ṛṣabham sūtaḥ uvāca provāca ca enam vinatā putra hārdāt idam vacaḥ jānanti api atulam vīryam āśīrvāda samanvitam pakṣau te mārutaḥ pātu candraḥ pṛṣṭham tu putraka aham ca te sadā putra śānti svasti parāyaṇā ariṣṭam vraja panthānam vatsa kārya artha siddhaye tatas niṣādān balavān upāgamat bubhukṣitaḥ kālaḥ iva antakaḥ mahān sa tān niṣādān upasaṃharan tadā samudra kukṣau ca viśoṣayan payaḥ samīpa gān bhūmidharān vicālayan tatas sa cakre mahat ānanam tadā niṣāda mārgam pratirudhya pakṣirāj tad ānanam vivṛtam atipramāṇa vat samabhyayuḥ gaganam iva arditāḥ khagāḥ sūtaḥ uvāca tasya kaṇṭham anuprāptaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ saha bhāryayā dahan dīptaḥ iva aṅgāraḥ tam uvāca antarikṣa gaḥ dvijottama vinirgaccha tūrṇam āsyāt apāvṛtāt na hi me brāhmaṇaḥ vadhyaḥ pāpeṣu api rataḥ sadā bruvāṇam evam garuḍam brāhmaṇaḥ samabhāṣata niṣādī mama bhāryā iyam nirgacchatu mayā saha garuḍaḥ uvāca etām api niṣādīm tvam parigṛhya āśu niṣpata tūrṇam saṃbhāvaya ātmānam ajīrṇam mama tejasā sūtaḥ uvāca tatas sa vipraḥ niṣkrāntaḥ niṣādī sahitaḥ tadā vardhayitvā ca garuḍam iṣṭam deśam jagāma ha vitatya pakṣau ākāśam utpapāta manaḥ javaḥ tatas apaśyat sa pitaram pṛṣṭaḥ ca ākhyātavān pituḥ mātuḥ dāsya vimokṣa artham āhariṣye tam adya vai mātrā ca asmi samādiṣṭaḥ niṣādān bhakṣaya iti vai yat bhuktvā amṛtam āhartum samarthaḥ syām aham prabho kaśyapaḥ uvāca āsīt vibhāvasuḥ nāma mahā ṛṣiḥ kopanaḥ bhṛśam bhrātā tasya anujaḥ ca āsīt supratīkaḥ mahā tapāḥ vibhāgam kīrtayati eva supratīkaḥ atha nityaśas athā bravīt ca tam bhrātā supratīkam vibhāvasuḥ tatas sva artha parān mūḍhān pṛthak bhūtān svakaiḥ dhanaiḥ viditvā bhedayanti etān amitrāḥ mitra rūpiṇaḥ bhinnānām atulaḥ nāśaḥ kṣipram eva pravartate tasmāt ca eva vibhāga artham na praśaṃsanti paṇḍitāḥ guru śāstre nibaddhānām anyonyam abhiśaṅkinām evam anyonya śāpāt tau supratīka vibhāvasū gaja kacchapatām prāptau artha artham mūḍha cetasau roṣa doṣa anuṣaṅgeṇa tiryagyoni gatau api sarasi asmin mahā kāyau pūrva vaira anusāriṇau tayoḥ ekataraḥ śrīmān samupaiti mahā gajaḥ tasya bṛṃhita śabdena kūrmaḥ api antar jaleśayaḥ utthitaḥ asau mahā kāyaḥ kṛtsnam saṃkṣobhayan saraḥ tam dṛṣṭvā āveṣṭita karaḥ patati eṣa gajaḥ jalam danta hasta agra lāṅgūla pāda vegena vīryavān tam vikṣobhayamāṇam tu saraḥ bahu jhaṣa ākulam kūrmaḥ api abhyudyata śirāḥ yuddhāya abhyeti vīryavān ṣaḍ ucchritaḥ yojanāni gajaḥ tat dviguṇa āyataḥ upayujya āśu karma idam sādhaya īpsitam ātmanaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca samutpapāta ca ākāśam tatas uccais vihaṃgamaḥ saḥ āsādya devavṛkṣān upāgamat te bhītāḥ samakampanta tasya pakṣa anila āhatāḥ na naḥ bhañjyāt iti tadā divyāḥ kanaka śākhinaḥ pracala aṅgān sa tān dṛṣṭvā manoratha phala aṅkurān anyān atula rūpa aṅgān upacakrāma khecaraḥ kāñcanaiḥ rājataiḥ ca eva phalaiḥ vaiḍūrya śākhinaḥ sāgara ambu parikṣiptān bhrājamānān mahā drumān tam uvāca khaga śreṣṭham tatra rohiṇa pādapaḥ yā eṣā mama mahā śākhā śata yojanam āyatā etām āsthāya śākhām tvam khāda imau gaja kacchapau sūtaḥ uvāca spṛṣṭa mātrā tu padbhyām sā garuḍena balīyasā abhajyata taroḥ śākhā bhagnām ca enām adhārayat tām bhagnām sa mahā śākhām smayan samavalokayan sa tad vināśa saṃtrāsāt anupatya khaga adhipaḥ śākhām āsyena jagrāha teṣām eva anvavekṣayā śanais paryapatat pakṣī parvatān praviśātayan dayā artham vālakhilyānām na ca sthānam avindata dadarśa tam pitā ca api divya rūpam vihaṃgamam śaila śṛṅga pratīkāśam brahmadaṇḍam iva udyatam māyā vīrya dharam sākṣāt agnim iddham iva udyatam apradhṛṣyam
